daityānāṃ vacanaṃ śrutvā dhunadhurdaityapurohitam 
papraccha śukraṃ kiṃ karma kṛtvā brahmasadogatiḥ  VamP 
tato 'smai kathayāmāsa daityacāryaḥ kalipriya 
śakrasya caritaṃ śrīmān purā vṛtraripoḥ kila  VamP 
śakraḥ śataṃ tu puṇyānāṃ krotūnāmajayat purā 
daityendra vājimedhānāṃ tena brahmasado gataḥ  VamP 
tadvākyaṃ dānavapatiḥ śrutvā śukrasya vīryavān 
yaṣṭuṃ turagamedhānāṃ cakāra matimuttamām 
athāmantryāsuraguruṃ dānavāṃścāpyanuttamān  VamP 
provāca yakṣye 'haṃ yajñairaśvamedhaiḥ sadakṣimaiḥ 
tadāgacchadhvamavanīṃ gacchāmo vasudhādhipān  VamP 
vijitya hayamedhān vai yathākāmaguṇanvinatān 
āhūyantāṃ ca nidhayastvājñāpyanātāṃ ca guhyakāḥ  VamP 
āmantryantāṃ ca ṛṣayaḥ prayāmo devikāṭatam 
sā hi puṇyā saricchreṣṭha sarvasiddhikarī śubhā 
sthānaṃ prācīnamāsādya vājisedhān yajāmahe  VamP 
itthaṃ surārervacanaṃ niśamyāsurayājakaḥ 
bāḍhamityabravīd hṛṣṭo nidhayaḥ saṃdideśa saḥ  VamP 
tato dhundhurdevikāyāḥ prācīne pāpanāśane 
bhārgavendreṇa śukreṇa vājimedhāya dīkṣitaḥ  VamP 
sadasyā ṛtvijaścāpi tatrāsan bhārgavā dvijāḥ 
śukrasyānumate brahman śukraśiṣyāśca paṇyitāḥ  VamP 
yajñabhāgabhujastatra svarbhānupramukhā mune 
kṛtāścāsuranāthena śukrasyānumate 'surāḥ  VamP 
tataḥ pravṛtto yajñastu samutsṛṣṭastathā hayaḥ 
hayasyānu yayau śrīmānasilomā mahāsuraḥ  VamP 
tato 'gnidhūmena mahī saśailā vyāptā diśaḥ khaṃ vidiśaśca pūrṇāḥ 
tenogragandhena divaspṛsena marud vavau brahmaloke maharṣe  VamP 
taṃ gandhamāghrāya surā viṣaṇṇā jānanta dhundhuṃ hayamedhadīkṣitam 
tataḥ śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇaṃ janārdhanaṃ jagmuḥ saśakrā jagātaḥ parayaṇam  VamP 
praṇamya varadaṃ devaṃ padmanābhaṃ janārdanam 
procuḥ sarve suragaṇā bhayagadgadayā girā  VamP 
bhagavan devadeveśa carācaraparāyaṇa 
vijñaptiḥ śrūyatāṃ viṣṇo surāṇāmārtināśana  VamP 
dhundhurnāmāsurapatirbalavān varabṛṃhitaḥ 
sarvān surān vinirjitya trailokyamahārad baliḥ  VamP 
ṛte pinākino devāt trāt'smān na yato hare 
ato vivṛddhimagamad yathā vyādhirupekṣitaḥ  VamP 
sāmprataṃ brahmalokasthānapi jetuṃ samudyataḥ 
śukrasya matamāstāya so 'śvamedhāya dīkṣitaḥ  VamP 
śataṃ kratūnāmiṣṭvāsau brahmalokaṃ mahāsuraḥ 
aroḍhumicchati vaśī vijetuṃ tridaśānapi  VamP 
tasmādakālahīnaṃ tu cintayasva jagadguro 
uvāyaṃ makhavidhvaṃse yena syāma sunirvṛtāḥ  VamP 
śrutvā surāṇāṃ vacanaṃ bhagavān madhusūdanaḥ 
dattvābhayaṃ mahābāhuḥ preṣayāmāsa sāmpratam 
visṛjya devatāḥ sarvā jñātvājeyaṃ mahāsuram  VamP 
bandhanāya matiṃ cakre dhundhordharmadhvajasya vai 
tataḥ kṛtvā sa bhagavān vāmanaṃ rūpamīśvaraḥ  VamP 
dehaṃ tyaktvā nirālambaṃ kāṣṭavad devikājale 
kṣaṇānmajjaṃstathonmajjanmuktakeśo yadṛcchayā  VamP 
dṛṣṭo 'tha daityapatinā daityaiścānyaistatharṣibhiḥ 
tataḥ karma parityajya yajñiyaṃ brāhmaṇottamāḥ  VamP 
samuttārayituṃ vipramādravanta samākulāḥ 
sadasyā yajamānaśca ṛtvijo 'tha mahaujasaḥ  VamP 
nimajjamānamujjahruḥ sarve te vāmanaṃ dvijam 
samuttārya prasannāste papracchuḥ sarva eva hi 
kimarthaṃ patito 'sīha kenākṣipto 'si no vada  VamP 
teṣāmākarṇya vacanaṃ kampamāno muhurmuhuḥ 
prāha dhundhupurogāṃstāñ chrūyatāmatra kāraṇam  VamP 
brāhmaṇo guṇavānāsīt prabhāsa iti viśrutaḥ 
sarvasāstrārthavit prājño gotrataś cāpi vāruṇaḥ  VamP 
tasya putradvayaṃ jātaṃ mandaprajñaṃ suduḥkhitam 
tatra jyeṣṭho mama bhrātā kanīyānaparastvaham  VamP 
netrabhāsa iti khyāto jyeṣṭho bhrātā mamāsura 
mama nāma pitā cakre gatibhāseti kautukāt  VamP 
ramyaścāvasatho bandho śubhaścāsīt piturmama 
triviṣṭapaguṇairyuktaścārurūpo mahāsura  VamP 
tataḥ kālena mahatā āvayoḥ sa pitā mṛtaḥ 
tasyordhvadehikaṃ kṛtvā gṛhamāvāṃ samāgatau  VamP 
tato mayoktaḥ sa bhrātā vibhajāma gṛhaṃ vayam 
tenokto naiva bhavato vidyate bhāgā ityaham  VamP 
kubjavāmanakhañjānāṃ klībānāṃ śvitriṇāmapi 
unmattānāṃ tathāndhānāṃ dhanabhāgo na vidyate  VamP 
śayyāsanasthānamātraṃ svecchayānnabhujakriyā 
etāvad dīyate tebhyo nārthabhāgaharā hi te  VamP 
evamukte mayā soktaḥ kimarthaṃ paitṛkād gṛhāt 
dhanārthabhāgamarhāmi nāhaṃ nyāyena kena vai  VamP 
ityuktāvati vākye 'sau bhrātā me kopasaṃyutaḥ 
samutkṣipyākṣipannadyāmasyāṃ māmiti kāraṇāt  VamP 
mamāsyāṃ nimnagāyāṃ tu madhyena plavato gataḥ 
kālaḥ saṃvatsarākhyastu yuṣmābhiriha coddhṛtaḥ  VamP 
ke bhavanto 'tra saṃprāptāḥ sasnehā bāndhavā iva 
ko 'yaṃ ca śakrapratimo dīkṣito yo mahābhujaḥ  VamP 
tanme sarvaṃ samākhyātā yāthātathyaṃ tapodhanāḥ 
maharddhisaṃyutā yūyaṃ sānukampāśca me bhṛśam  VamP 
tad vāmanavacaḥ śrutvā bhārgavā dvijasattamāḥ 
procurvaṃ dvijā brahman gotraścāpi bhārgavāḥ  VamP 
asāvapi mahātejā dhundhurnāma mahāsuraḥ 
dātā bhoktā vibhaktā ca dīkṣito yajñakarmaṇi  VamP 
ityevamuktvā deveśaṃ vāmanaṃ bhārgavāstataḥ 
procurdaityapatiṃ sarve vāmanārthakaraṃ vacaḥ  VamP 
dīyatāmasya daityendra sarvopaskarasaṃyutam 
śrīmadāvasathaṃ dāsyo ratnāni vividhāni ca  VamP 
iti dvijānāṃ vacanaṃ śrutvā daityapatirvacaḥ 
prāha dvijendra te dadmi yāvadicchasi vai dhanam  VamP 
dāste gṛhaṃ hiraṇyaṃ ca vājinaḥ syandanān gajān 
prayacchāmyadya bhavato vriyatāmīpsitaṃ vibho  VamP 
tadvākyaṃ dānavapateḥ śrutvā devo 'tha vāmanaḥ 
prāhāsurapatiṃ dhundhuṃ svārthasiddhikaraṃ vacaḥ  VamP 
sodareṇāpi hi bhrātrā hriyante yasya saṃpadaḥ 
tasyākṣamasya yaddattaṃ kimanyo na hariṣyati  VamP 
dāsīdāsāṃśca bhṛtyāṃśca gṛhaṃ ratnaṃ paricchadam 
samartheṣu dvijendreṣu prayacchasva mahābhuja  VamP 
mama pramāṇamālokya māmakaṃ ca padatrayam 
saṃprayacchasva daityendra nādhikaṃ rakṣituṃ kṣamaḥ  VamP 
ityevamukte vacane mahātmanā vihasya daityādhipatiḥ saṛtvijaḥ 
prādād dvijendrāya padatrayaṃ tadā yadā sa nānyaṃ pragṛhāṇa kiñcit  VamP 
kramatrayaṃ tāvadavekṣya dattaṃ mahāsurendreṇa vibhuryaśasvī 
cakre tato laṅghayituṃ trivikramaṃ rūpamanantaśaktiḥ  VamP 
kṛtvā ca rūpaṃ ditijāṃśca hatvā praṇamya carṣin prathamakrameṇa 
mahīṃ mahīdhraiḥ sahitāṃ sahārmavāṃ jahāra ratnākarapattanairyutām  VamP 
bhuvaṃ sanākaṃ tridasādhivāsaṃ somārkaṛkṣair abhimaṇḍitaṃ nabhaḥ 
devo dvitīyena jahāra vegāt krameṇa devapriyamīpsurīśvaraḥ  VamP 
kramaṃ tṛtīyaṃ na yadāsya pūritaṃ tadātikopād danupuṅgavasya 
papāta pṛṣṭhe bhagavāṃstrivikramo merupramāṇena tu vigraheṇa  VamP 
patatā vāsudevena dānavopari nārada 
triṃśadyojanasāhasrī bhūmergartā dṛḍhīkṛtā  VamP 
tato daityaṃ samutpāṭya tasyāṃ prakṣipya vegataḥ 
avarṣat sikatāvṛṣṭyā tāṃ gartāmapūrayata  VamP 
tataḥ svargaṃ sahasrākṣo vāsudevaprasādataḥ 
surāśca sarve trailokyamavāpurnirupadravāḥ  VamP 
bhagavānapi daityendraṃ pakṣipya sikatārṇave 
kālindya rūpamādhāya tatraivāntaradhīyata  VamP 
evaṃ purā viṣṇurabhūcca vāmano dhundhuṃ vijetuṃ ca trivikramo 'bhūt 
yasmin sa daityendrasuto jagāma mahāśrame puṇyayuto maharṣe  VamP 
iti śrīvāmanapurāṇe dvipañcāśo 'dhyāyaḥ
pulastya uvāca 
kālindīsalile snātvā pūjayitvā trivikramam 
upoṣya rajanīmekāṃ liṅgabhedaṃ giriṃ yayau  VamP 
tatra snātvā ca vimale bhavaṃ dṛṣṭvā ca bhaktitaḥ 
upoṣya rajanīmekāṃ tīrthaṃ kedāramāvrajat  VamP 
tatra snātvār'cya ceśānaṃ mādhavaṃ cāpyabhedataḥ 
uṣitvā vāsarān sapta kubjāmraṃ prajagāma ha  VamP 
tataḥ sutīrthe snātvā ca sopavāsī jitendriyaḥ hṛṣīkeśaṃ samabhyarcya yayau badarikāśramam  VamP 
tatroṣya nārāyaṇamarcya bhaktyā snātvātha vidvān sa sarasvatījale 
varāhatīrthe garuḍāsanaṃ sa dṛṣṭvātha saṃpūjya subhaktimāṃśca  VamP 
bhadrakarṇe tato gatvā jayeśaṃ śaśiśekharam 
dṛṣṭvā saṃpūjya ca śivaṃ vipāśāmabhito yayau  VamP 
tasyāṃ snātvā samabhyarcya devadevaṃ dvijapriyam 
upavāsī irāvatyāṃ dadarśa parameśvaram  VamP 
yamārādhya dvijaśreṣṭha śākale vai purūravāḥ 
samavāpa paraṃ rūpamaiśvarya ca sudurlabham  VamP 
kuṣṭharogābhibhūtaśca yaṃ samārāghya vai bhṛguḥ 
ārogyamatulaṃ prāpa saṃtānamapi cākṣayam  VamP 
nārada uvāca 
kathaṃ purūravā viṣṇumārāghya dvijasattama 
virūpatvaṃ samutsṛjya rūpaṃ prāpa śriyā saha  VamP 
pulastya uvāca 
śrūyatāṃ kathayiṣyāmi kathāṃ pāpupraṇāśinīm 
pūrvaṃ tretāyugasyādau yathāvṛttaṃ tapodhana  VamP 
madradeśa iti khyāto deśo vai brahmaṇaḥ suta 
śākalaṃ nāma nagaraṃ khyātaṃ sthānīyamuttamam  VamP 
tasmin vipaṇivṛttisthaḥ sudharmākhyo 'bhavad vaṇik 
dhanāḍhyo guṇavān bhogī nānāsāstraviśāradaḥ  VamP 
sa tvekadā nijād rāṣṭrāt surāṣṭraṃ gantumadyataḥ 
sārthena mahatā yukto nānāvipaṇapaṇyavān  VamP 
gacchataḥ pathi tasyātha marubhūmau kalipriya 
abhavad dasyuto rātrau avaskando 'tiduḥsahaḥ  VamP 
tataḥ sa hṛtasarvasvo vaṇig guḥkhasamanvitaḥ 
asahāyo marau tasmiṃś cacāronmattavad vaśī  VamP 
caratā tadaraṇyaṃ vai duḥkhākrāntena nārada 
ātmā iva śamīvṛkṣo marāvāsāditaḥ śubhaḥ  VamP 
taṃ mṛgauḥ pikṣikṣiścaiva hīnaṃ dṛṣṭvā śamītarum 
śrāntaḥ kṣuttṛṭparītātmā tasyādhaḥ samupāviśat  VamP 
suptaścāpi suviśrānto madhyāhne punarutyitaḥ 
samapaśyadathāyāntaṃ pretaṃ pretaśatairvṛtam  VamP 
udvāhyantamathānyena pretena pretanāyakam 
piṇḍāśibhiśca purato dhāvadbhī rūkṣavigrahaiḥ  VamP 
athājagāma preto 'sau paryaṭitvā vanāni ca 
upāgamya śamīmūle vaṇikputraṃ dadarśa saḥ  VamP 
svāgatenābhivādyainaṃ samābhāṣya parasparam 
sukhopaviṣṭaśchāyāyāṃ pṛṣṭvā kuśalamāptavān  VamP 
tataḥ pretādhipatinā pṛṣṭaḥ sa tu vaṇiksakhaḥ 
kuta āgamyate brūhi kva sādho vā gamiṣyasi  VamP 
kathaṃ cedaṃ mahāraṇyaṃ mṛgapakṣivivarjitam 
samāpanno 'si bhadraṃ te sarvamākhyātumarhasi  VamP 
evaṃ pretādhipatinā vaṇik pṛṣṭaḥ samāsataḥ 
sarvamākhyātavān brahman svadeśadhanavicyutim  VamP 
tasya śrutvā sa vṛttāntaṃ tasya duḥkhena duḥkhitaḥ 
vamikputraṃ tataḥ prāha pretapālaḥ svabandhuvat  VamP 
evaṃ gate 'pi mā śokaṃ kartumarhasi suvrata 
bhūyo 'pyarthāḥ bhaviṣyanti yadi bhāgyabalaṃ tava  VamP 
bhāgyakṣayer'thāḥ kṣīyante bhavantyabhyudaye punaḥ 
kṣīṇasyāsya śarīrasya cintayā nodayo bhavet  VamP 
ityuccārya samāhūya svān bhṛtyān vākyamabravīt 
adyātithirayaṃ pūjyaḥ sadaiva svajano mama  VamP 
asmin samāgate pretāḥ prītirjātā mamātulā  VamP 
evaṃ hi vadatastasya mṛtpātraṃ sudṛḍhaṃ navam 
dadhyodanena saṃpūrṇamājagāma yathepsitam  VamP 
tathā navā ca sudṛḍhā saṃpūrṇā paramāmbhasā 
vāridhānī ca saṃprāptā pretānāmagrataḥ sthitā  VamP 
tamāgataṃ sasalilamannaṃ vīkṣya mahāmatiḥ 
prāhottiṣṭha vaṇikputra tvamāhnikamupācara  VamP 
tatastu vāridhānyāstau salilena vidhānataḥ 
kṛtāhnikāvubhau jātau vaṇik pretapatistathā  VamP 
tato vaṇiksutāyādau dadhyodanamathecchayā 
dattvā tebhyaśca sarvebhyaḥ pretebhyo vyadadāt tataḥ  VamP 
bhuktavatsu ca sarveṣu kāmato 'mbhasi sevite 
anantaraṃ sabubhuje pretapālo barāśanam  VamP 
prakāmatṛpte preta ca vāridhānyodanaṃ tathā 
antardhānamagād brahman vaṇikputrasya paśyataḥ  VamP 
tatastadadbhutatamaṃ dṛṣṭvā sa matimān vaṇik 
papraccha taṃ pretapālaṃ kautūhalamanā vaśī  VamP 
araṇye nirjane sādho kuto 'nnasya samudbhavaḥ 
kutaśca vāridhānīyaṃ saṃpūrṇā paramāmbhasā  VamP 
tathāmī tava ye bhṛtyāstvattaste varmataḥ kṛśāḥ 
bhavānapi ca tejasvī kiñcitpuṣṭavapuḥ śubhaḥ  VamP 
śuklavastraparīdhāno bahūnāṃ paripālakaḥ 
sarvametanmamācakṣva ko bhavān kā śamī tviyam  VamP 
itthaṃ vaṇiksutavacaḥ śrutvāsau pretanāyakaḥ 
śaśaṃsa sarvamasyādyaṃ yathāvṛttaṃ purātanam  VamP 
ahamāsaṃ purā vipraḥ śākale nagarottame 
somaśarmeti vikhyāto bahulāgarbhasaṃbhavaḥ  VamP 
mamāsti ca vaṇik śrīmān prāti veśyo mahādhanaḥ 
sa tu somaśravā nāma viṣṇubhakto mahāyaśāḥ  VamP 
so 'haṃ kadaryo mūḍhātmā dhane 'pi sati durmatiḥ 
na dadāmi dvijātibhyo na cāśnāmyannamuttamam  VamP 
pramādād yadi bhuñjāmi dadhikṣīraghṛtānvitam 
tato rātrau nṛbhir ghoraistāḍyate mama vigrahaḥ  VamP 
prātarbhavati me ghorā mṛtyutulyā viṣūcikā 
na ca kaścinmābhyāse tatra tiṣṭhati bāndhavaḥ  VamP 
kathaṃ kathamapi prāṇā mayā saṃpratidhāritāḥ 
evametādṛśaḥ pāpī nivasāmyatinirghṛṇaḥ  VamP 
sauvīratilapiṇyākasaktuśākādibhonaiḥ 
kṣapayāmi kadannādyairātmānaṃ kālayāpanaiḥ  VamP 
evaṃ tatrāsato mahyaṃ mahān kālo 'bhyagādatha 
śravaṇadvādaśī nāma māsi bhādrapade 'bhavat  VamP 
tato nāgariko loko gataḥ snātuṃ hi saṃgamam 
irāvatyā naḍvalāyā brahmakṣatrapurassaraḥ  VamP 
prātiveśyaprasaṃgena tatrāpyanugato 'smyaham 
kṛtopavāsaḥ śucimānekādaśyāṃ yatavrataḥ  VamP 
tataḥ saṃgamatoyena vāridhānīṃ dṛḍhāṃ navām 
saṃpūrṇāṃ vastusaṃvītāṃ chatropānahasaṃyutām  VamP 
sṛtpātramapi miṣṭasya pūrṇaṃ dadhyodanasya ha 
pradattaṃ brāhmaṇendrāya śucaye jñānadharmiṇe  VamP 
tadeva jīvatā dattaṃ mayā dānaṃ vaṇiksuta 
varṣāṇāṃ saptatīnāṃ vai nānyad dattaṃ hi kiñcana  VamP 
mṛtaḥ pretatvamāpanno dattvā pretānnameva hi 
amī cādattadānāstu madannenopajīvinaḥ  VamP 
etate kāraṇaṃ proktaṃ yattadannaṃ mayāmbhasā 
dattaṃ tadidamāyāti madhyāhne 'pi dine dine  VamP 
yāvannāhaṃ ca bhuñjāmi na tāvat kṣayameti vai 
mayi bhukte ca pīte ca sarvamantarhitaṃ bhavet  VamP 
yaccātapatramadadaṃ so 'yaṃ jātaḥ śamītaruḥ 
uvānadyugale datte preto me vāhano 'bhavat  VamP 
iyaṃ tovaktā dharmajña mayā kīnāśatātmanaḥ 
śravaṇadvādaśīpuṇyaṃ tavokyaṃ puṇayavardharam  VamP 
ityevamukte vacane vaṇikputro 'bravīd vacaḥ 
yanmayā tāta karttavyaṃ tadanujñātumarhasi  VamP 
tat tasya vacanaṃ śrutvā vaṇikputrasya nārada 
pretapālo vacaḥ prāha svārthasiddhikaraṃ tataḥ  VamP 
yat tvayā tāta karttavyaṃ maddhitārthaṃ mahāmate 
kathayiṣyāmi tat samyak tava śreyaskaraṃ mama  VamP 
gayāyāṃ tīrthajuṣṭāyāṃ snātvā śaucasamanvitaḥ 
mama nāma samuddiśya piṇḍanirvapaṇaṃ kuru  VamP 
tatra piṇḍapradānena pretabhāvādahaṃ sakhe 
muktastu sarvadātṛṇāṃ yāsyāmi sahalokatām  VamP 
yatheyaṃ dvādaśī puṇyā māsi prauṣṭhapade sitā 
budhaśravaṇasaṃyuktā sātiśreyaskarī smṛtā  VamP 
ityevamuktvā vaṇijaṃ pretarājo 'nugaiḥ saha 
svanāmāni yathānyāyaṃ samyagākhyātavāñchuciḥ  VamP 
pretaskandhe samāropya tyājito marumaṇḍalam 
ramye 'tha śūrasenākhye deśe prāptaḥ sa vai vaṇik  VamP 
svakarmadharmayogena dhanamuccāvacaṃ bahu 
uvārjayitvā prayayau gayāśīrṣamanuttamam  VamP 
piṇḍanirvapaṇaṃ tatra pretānāmanupūrvaśaḥ 
cakāra svapitṝṇāṃ ca dāyādānāmanantaram  VamP 
ātmanaśca mahābuddhirmahābodhyaṃ tilairvinā 
piṇḍanirvapaṇaṃ cakre tathānyānapi gotrajān  VamP 
evaṃ pradatteṣvatha vai piṇḍeṣu pretabhāvataḥ 
vimuktāste dvija pretā brahmalokaṃ tato gatāḥ  VamP 
sa cāpi hi vaṇikputro nijamālayamāvrajat 
śravaṇadvādaśīṃ kṛtvā kāladharmamupeyivān  VamP 
gandharvaloke suciraṃ bhogān bhuktvā sudurlabhān 
mānuṣyaṃ janmamāsādya sa babhau śākale virāṭ  VamP 
svadharmakarmavṛttisthaḥ śravaṇadvādaśīrataḥ 
kāladharmamavāpyāsau guhyakāvāsamāśrayat  VamP 
tatroṣya suciraṃ kālaṃ bhogān bhuktvātha kāmataḥ 
martyalokamanuprāpya rājanyatanayo 'bhavat  VamP 
tatrāpi kṣatravṛttistho dānabhogarato vaśī 
gograhe 'rigaṇāñjitvā kāladharmamupeyivān 
śakralokaṃ sa saṃprāpya devaiḥ sarvaiḥ supūjitaḥ  VamP 
puṇyakṣayāt paribhraṣṭaḥ śākale so 'bhavad dvijaḥ 
tato vikaṭarūpo 'sau sarvaśāstrārthapāragaḥ  VamP 
vivāhayad dvijasutāṃ rūpeṇānupamāṃ dvija

surūpatāmavāpyāgryāṃ tasminneva ca janmani 
tataḥ priyo 'bhūd bhāryāyā bhogavāṃścābhavad vaśī 
śravaṇadvādaśībhaktaḥ pūrvābhyāsādajāyata  VamP

iti śrīvāmanapurāṇe tripañcāśo 'dhyāyaḥ
nārada uvāca 
purūravā dvijaśreṣṭha yathā devaṃ śriyaḥ patim 
nakṣatrapuruṣākhyena ārādhayata tad vada  VamP 
pulastya uvāca 
śrūyatāṃ kathayiṣyāmi nakṣatrapuruṣavratam 
nakṣatrāṅgani devasya yāni yānīha nārada  VamP 
mūlarkṣaṃ caraṇau viṣṇorjaṅghe dve rohiṇī smṛte

āṣāḍhaṃ dve dvayaṃ corvorguhyasthaṃ phālgunīdvayam 
kaṭisthāḥ kṛttikāścaiva vāsudevasya saṃsthitāḥ  VamP 
prauṣṭhapadyādvayaṃ pārśve kukṣibhyāṃ revatī sthitā

hanū dve vāruṇaścokto nāsā paitra udāhṛtaḥ

nakṣatrasannidhau dadyād viprendrāya ca bhojanam  VamP

devendravighnaśamanodyatapauruṣāya yogeśvarāya virajāya namo varāya  VamP

nārāyaṇāyātmahitāyanāya mahāvarāhāya namaskaromi  VamP 
kūṭasthamavyaktamacintyarūpaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ kāraṇamādidevam 
yugāntaśeṣaṃ puruṣaṃ purāṇaṃ taṃ devadevaṃ śaraṇaṃ prapadye  VamP 
yogeśvaraṃ cāruvicitramaulim ajñeyam agryaṃ prakṛteḥ parastham 
kṣetrajñamātmaprabhavaṃ vareṇyaṃ taṃ vāsudevaṃ śaraṇaṃ prapadya  VamP 
adṛśyamavyaktamacintyamavyayaṃ maharṣayo brahmayaṃ sanātanam 
vadanti yaṃ vai puruṣaṃ sanātanaṃ taṃ devaguhyaṃ śaraṇaṃ prapadye  VamP 
yadakṣaraṃ brahma vadanti sarvagaṃ niśamya yaṃ mṛtyumukhāt pramucyate 
tamīśvaraṃ tṛptamanuttamairguṇaiḥ parāyaṇaṃ viṣṇumupaimi sāśvatam  VamP 
kāryaṃ kriyā kāraṇamaprameyaṃ hiraṇyabāhuṃ varapadmanābham 
mahābalaṃ vedanidhiṃ sureśaṃ vajāmi viṣṇuṃ śaraṇaṃ janārdanam  VamP 
kirīṭakeyūramahārhaniṣkairmaṇyuttamālaṅkṛtasarvagātram 
pītāmbaraṃ kāñcanabhakticitraṃ mālādharaṃ keśavamabhyupaimi  VamP 
bhavodbhavaṃ vedavidāṃ pariṣṭhaṃ yogātmanāṃ sāṃkhyavidāṃ variṣṭham 
ādityarudrāśvivasuprabhāvaṃ prabhuṃ prapadye 'cyutamātmavantam  VamP 
śrīvatsāṅkaṃ mahādevaṃ devaguhyamanaupamam 
prapadye sūkṣmamacalaṃ vareṇyamabhayapradam  VamP 
prabhavaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ nirguṇaṃ parameśvaram 
prapadye muktasaṃgānāṃ yatīnāṃ paramāṃ gatim  VamP 
bhagavantaṃ guṇādhyakṣamakṣaraṃ puṣkarekṣaṇam 
śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇaṃ bhaktyā prapadye bhaktavatsalam  VamP 
trivikramaṃ trilokeśaṃ sarveṣāṃ prapitāmaham 
yogātmānaṃ mahātmānaṃ prapadye 'haṃ janārdanam  VamP 
ādidevamajaṃ śaṃbhuṃ vyaktāvyaktaṃ sanātanam 
nārāyaṇamaṇīyāṃsaṃ prapadye brāhmaṇapriyam  VamP 
namo varāya devāya namaḥ sarvasahāya ca 
prapadye devadeveśamaṇīyāṃsamaṇoḥ sadā  VamP 
ekāya lokattvāya parataḥ paramātmane 
namaḥ sahasraśirase anantāya mahātmane  VamP 
tvāmeva paramaṃ devamṛṣayo vedapāragāḥ 
kīrtayanti ca yaṃ sarve brahmādīnāṃ parāyaṇam  VamP 
namaste puṇḍarīkākṣa bhaktānāmabhayaprada 
subrahmaṇya namaste 'stu trāhi māṃ śaraṇāgatam  VamP 
pulastya uvāca 
bhaktiṃ tasyānusaṃcintya nāgasyamoghasaṃbhavaḥ 
prītimānabhavad viṣṇuḥ śaṅkhacakragadādharaḥ  VamP 
sānnidhyaṃ kalpayāmāsa tasmin sarasi keśavaḥ 
garuḍastho jagatsvāmī lokādhārastapodhanaḥ  VamP 
grāhagrastaṃ gajendraṃ taṃ taṃ ca grāhaṃ jalāśayāt 
ujjahārāprameyātmā tarasā madhusūdanaḥ  VamP 
sthalasthaṃ dārayāmāsa grāhaṃ cakreṇa mādhavaḥ 
mokṣayāmāsa nāgendraṃ pāśebhyaḥ śaraṇāgatam  VamP 
sa hi devalaśāpena hūhūrgandharvasattamaḥ 
grāhatvamagamat kṛṣṇād vadhaṃ prāpya divaṃ gataḥ  VamP 
gajo 'pi viṣṇunā spṛṣṭo jāto divyavapuḥ pumān 
āpadviktau yugapad gajagandharvasattamau  VamP 
prītīmān puṇḍarīkākṣaḥ śaraṇāgatavatsalaḥ 
abhavat tvatha deveśastābhyāṃ caiva prapūjitaḥ  VamP 
idaṃ ca bhagavān yogī gajendraṃ śaraṇāgatam 
provāca muniśārdūla madhuraṃ madhusūdanaḥ  VamP  
śrībhagavānuvāca 
yo māṃ tvāñca saraścaiva grāhasya ca vidāraṇam 
gulmakīcakareṇūnāṃ rūpaṃ meroḥ sutasya ca  
 aśvatthaṃ bhāskaraṃ gaṅgaṃ naimiṣāraṇyameva ca 
saṃsmariṣyanti manujāḥ prayatāḥ sthirabuddhayaḥ  VamP 
kīrtayiṣyanti bhaktyā ca śroṣyanti ca śucivrataḥ 
duḥsvapno naśyate teṣāṃ susvapnaśca bhaviṣyati  VamP 
mātsyaṃ kaurmañca vārāhaṃ vāmanaṃ tārkṣyameva ca 
nārasiṃhaṃ ca nāgendraṃ sṛṣṭipralayakārakam  VamP 
etāni prātarutthāya saṃsmariṣyanati ye narāḥ 
sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyante puṇyaṃ lokamavāpnuyuḥ  VamP 
pulastya uvāca 
evamuktvā hṛṣīkeśo gajendraṃ garuḍadhvajaḥ 
sparśayāmāsa hastena gajaṃ gandharvameva ca  VamP 
tato divyavapurbhatvā gajendro madhusūdanam 
jagāma śaraṇaṃ vipra nārāyaṇaparāyamaḥ  VamP 
tato nārāyaṇaḥ śrīmān mokṣayitvā gajottamam 
pāpabanadhācca śāpācca grāhaṃ cādbhutakarmakṛt  VamP 
ṛṣibhiḥ stūyamānaśca devaguhyaparāyaṇaiḥ 
gataḥ sa bhagavān viṣṇurdurvijñeyagatiḥ prabhuḥ  VamP 
gajendramokṣaṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā devāḥ śakrapurogamāḥ 
vavandire mahātmānaṃ prabhuṃ nārāyaṇaṃ harim  VamP 
maharṣayaścāraṇāśca dṛṣṭvā gajavimokṣaṇam 
vismayotphūllanayanāḥ saṃstuvanti janārdanam  VamP 
prajāpatipatirbrahmā cakrapāṇiviceṣṭitam 
gajendramokṣaṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā idaṃ vacanamabravīt  VamP 
ya idaṃ śṛṇuyāntityaṃ prātarutthāya mānavaḥ 
prāpnuyāt paramāṃ siddhiṃ duḥsvapnastasya naśyati  VamP 
gajendra mokṣaṇaṃ puṇyaṃ sarvapāpapraṇāśanam 
kathitena smṛtenātha śrutena ca tapodhanaḥ 
gajendramokṣaṇeneha sadyaḥ pāpāt pramucyate  VamP 
etatpavitraṃ paramaṃ supuṇyaṃ saṃkīrtanīyaṃ caritaṃ murāreḥ 
yasmin kilokte bahupāpabandhanāt labhyeta mokṣo dviradena yadvat  VamP 
ajaṃ vareṇyaṃ varapadmanābhaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ brahmanidhiṃ sureśam 
taṃ devaguhyaṃ puruṣaṃ purāṇaṃ vandāmyahaṃ lokapatiṃ vareṇyam  VamP 
pulastya uvāca 
etat tavoktaṃ pravaraṃ stavānāṃ stavaṃ murārervaranāgakīrtanam 
yaṃ kīrtya saṃśrutya tathā vicintya pāpāpanodaṃ puruṣo labheta  VamP 
iti śrīvāmanapurāṇe aṣṭapañcāśo 'dhyāyaḥ
pulastya uvāca 
kaścidāsīd dvijadrogdhā piśunaḥ kṣatriyādhamaḥ 
parapīḍāruciḥ kṣudraḥ svabhāvādapi nirghṛṇaḥ  VamP 
paryāsitāḥ dā tena pitṛdevadvijātayaḥ 
sa tvāyuṣi parikṣiṇe jajñe ghoro niśācaraḥ  VamP 
tenaiva karmadoṣema svena pāpakṛtāṃ varaḥ 
kruraiścakre tato vṛttiṃ rākṣasatvād viśeṣataḥ  VamP 
tasya pāparatasyaivaṃ jagmurvarṣaśatāni tu 
tenaiva karmadoṣeṇa nānyāṃ vṛttimarocayat  VamP 
yaṃ yaṃ paśyati sattvaṃ sa taṃ tamādāya rākṣasaḥ 
cakhāda raudrakarmāsau bāhugocaramāgatam  VamP 
evaṃ tasyātiduṣṭasya kurvataḥ prāṇināṃ vadham 
jagāma ca mahān kālaḥ pariṇāmaṃ tathā vayaḥ  VamP 
sa kadācit tapasyantaṃ dadarśa sataritastaṭe 
mahābhāgamūrdhvabhujaṃ yathāvatsaṃyatendriyam  VamP 
anayā rakṣayā brahman kṛtarakṣaṃ taponidhim 
yogācāryaṃ śuciṃ dakṣaṃ vāsudevaparāyaṇam  VamP 
viṣṇuḥ prācyāṃ stitaścakrī viṣaṇurdakṣiṇato gadī 
pratīcyāṃ śārṅgadhṛgviṣṇurviṣṇuḥ khaḍgī mamottare  VamP 
hṛṣīkeśo vikoṇeṣu tacchidreṣu janārdanaḥ 
kroḍarūpī harirbhūmau nārasiṃho 'mbare mama  VamP 
śrurāntamamalaṃ cakraṃ bhramatyetat sudarśanam 
asyāṃśumālā duṣprekṣyā hantuṃ pretaniśācarān  VamP 
gadā ceyaṃ sahasrārcirudvaman pāvako yathā 
rakṣobhūtapiśācānāṃ ḍākinīnāṃ ca śātanī  VamP 
śārṅgaṃ visphūrjitaṃ caiva vāsudevasya madripūn 
tiryaṅmanuṣyakūṣmāṇḍapretādīn hantvaśeṣataḥ  VamP 
khaḍgadhārājvalajjyotsnānirdhūtā ye mamāhitāḥ 
te yāntu saumyatāṃ sadyo garuḍeneva pannagāḥ  VamP 
ye kūṣmāṇḍāstathā yakṣā daityā ye ca niśācarāḥ 
pretā vināyakāḥ krūrā manuṣyā jṛmbhakāḥ khagāḥ  VamP 
siṃhādayo ye paśavo dandaśūkāśca pannagāḥ 
sarve bhavantu me saumyā viṣṇucakraravāhatāḥ  VamP 
cittavṛttiharā ye ca ye janāḥ smṛtīhārakāḥ 
balaujasāṃ ca hartāraśchāyāvidhvaṃsakāśca ye  VamP 
ye copabhogahartāro ye ca lakṣaṇanāśakāḥ 
kūṣmāṇḍāste praṇaśyantu viṣṇucakraravāhatāḥ  VamP 
buddhisvāsthyaṃ manaḥsvāsthyaṃ svāsthamaindriyakaṃ tathā 
mamāstu devadevasya vāsudevasya kīrtanāt  VamP 
pṛṣṭhe purastādatha dakṣiṇottare vikoṇataścāstu najārdano hariḥ 
tamīḍyamīśānamanantamacyutaṃ janārdanaṃ praṇipatito na sīdati  VamP 
yathā paraṃ brahma haristathā paraṃ jagatsvarūpaśca sa eva keśavaḥ 
ṛtena tenācyutanāmakīrtanātpraṇāśametu trividhaṃ mamāsubham  VamP 
ityasāvātmarakṣārthaṃ kṛtvā vai viṣṇupañjaram 
saṃsthito 'sāvapi balī rākṣasaḥ samupādravat  VamP 
tato dvijaniyuktāyāṃ rakṣāyāṃ rajanīcaraḥ 
nirdhūtavegaḥ sahasā tasthau māsacatuṣṭayam  VamP 
yāvad dvijasya devarṣe samāptirvai samādhitaḥ 
jāte japyāvasāne 'sau ta dadarśa niśācaram  VamP 
dīnaṃ hatabālotsāhaṃ kāndiśīkaṃ hataujasam 
taṃ dṛṣṭvā kṛpayāviṣṭaḥ samāśvāsya niśācaram  VamP 
papracchāgamane hetuṃ sa cācaṣṭa yathātatham 
svabhāvamātmano draṣṭuṃ rakṣayā tejasaḥ kṣitim  VamP 
kathayitvā ca tadrakṣaḥ kāraṇaṃ vividhaṃ tataḥ 
prasīdetyabravīd vipraṃ nirviṇṇāḥ svena karmaṇā  VamP 
bahūni pāpāni mokṣamicchāmi tvatprasādataḥ 
kṛtāḥ striyo mayā bahvyo vidhavāḥ putravarjitāḥ 
anāgasāṃ ca sattvānāmalpakānāṃ kṣayaḥ kṛtaḥ  VamP 
tasmāt pāpādahaṃ mokṣamicchami tvatprasādataḥ 
pāpapraśamanāyālaṃ kuru me dharmadeśanam  VamP 
pāpasyāsya kṣayaramupadeśaṃ prayaccha me 
tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā rākṣasasya dvijottamaḥ  VamP 
vacanaṃ prāha dharmātmā hetumacca subhāṣitam 
kathaṃ krūrasvabhāvasya satastava niśācara 
sahasaiva samāyātā jijñāsā dharmavartmani  VamP 
rākṣasa uvāca 
tvāṃ vai samāgato 'smyadya kṣipto 'haṃ rakṣayā balāt 
tava saṃsargato brahman jāto nirveda uttamaḥ  VamP 
kā sā rakṣā na tāṃ vedmi vedmi nāsyāḥ parāyaṇam 
yasyāḥ saṃsargasāsādya nirvedaṃ prāpitaṃ param  VamP 
tvaṃ kṛpāṃ kuru dharmajña mayyanukrośamāvaha 
yathā pāpāpanodo me bhavatyārya tathā kuru  VamP 
pulastya uvāca 
ityevamuktaḥ sa munistadā vai tena rakṣasā 
pratyuvāca mahābhāgo vimṛśya suciraṃ muniḥ  VamP 
ṛṣiruvāca 
yanmamāhopadeśārthaṃ nirviṇṇāḥ svena karmaṇā 
yuktametaddhi pāpānāṃ nivṛttirupakārikā  VamP 
kariṣye yātudhānānāṃ natvahaṃ dharmadeśanam 
tān saṃpṛccha dvijān saumya ye vai pravacane ratāḥ  VamP 
evamuktvā yayau vipraścintāmāpa sa rākṣasaḥ 
kathaṃ pāpāpanodaḥ syāditi cintākulendriyaḥ  VamP 
na cakhāda sa sattvāni kṣudhā saṃbādhito 'pi san 
ṣaṣṭhe ṣaṣṭhe tadā kāle jantumekamabhakṣayat  VamP 
sa kadācitkṣudhāviṣṭaḥ paryaṭan vipule vane 
dadarśātha phalāhāramāgataṃ brahmacāriṇam   
gṛhīto rakṣasā tena sa tadā munidārakaḥ 
nirāśo jīvite prāha sāmapūrvaṃ niśācaram  VamP 
brāhmaṇa uvāca 
bho bhadra brūhi yat kāryaṃ gṛhīto yena hetunā 
tadanubrūhi bhadraṃ te ayamasmyanuśādhi mām  VamP 
rākṣasa uvāca 
ṣaṣṭhe kāle tvamāhāraḥ kṣudhitasya samāgataḥ 
niḥśrīkasyātipāpasya nirghṛṇasya dvijadruhaḥ  VamP 
brāhmaṇa uvāca 
yadyavaśyaṃ tvayā cāhaṃ bhakṣitavyo niśācara 
āyāsyāmi tavādyaiva nivedya gurave phalam  VamP 
gurvarthametadāgatya yatphalagrahaṇaṃ kṛtam 
mamātra niṣṭhā prāptasya phalāni viniveditum  VamP 
sa tvaṃ muhūrtamātraṃ māmatraivaṃ pratipālaya 
nivedya gurave yāvadihāgacchāmyahaṃ phalam  VamP 
rākṣasa uvāca 
ṣaṣṭhe kāle na me brahman kaścid grahaṇamāgataḥ 
pratimucyeta devo 'pi iti me pāpājīvikā  VamP 
eka evātra mokṣasya tava hetuḥ śṛṇuṣva tat 
muñcāmyahamasaṃdigdhaṃ yadi tatkurute bhavān  VamP 
brāhmaṇa uvāca 
guroryanna virodhāya yanna dharmoparodhakam 
tatkariṣyāmyahaṃ rakṣo yanna vrataharaṃ mama  VamP 
rākṣasa uvāca 
mayā nisargato brahman jātidoṣād viśeṣataḥ 
nirvivekena cittena pāpakarma sadā kṛtam  VamP 
ābālyānmama pāpeṣu na dharmeṣu rataṃ manaḥ 
tatpāpāsaṃkṣayānmokṣaṃ prāpnuyāṃ yena tad vada  VamP 
yāni pāpāni karmāṇi bālatvāccaritāni ca 
duṣṭāṃ yonimimāṃ prāpya tanmuktiṃ kathaya dvija  VamP 
yadyetad dvijaputra tvaṃ samākhyāsyasyaśeṣataḥ 
tataḥ kṣudhārtānmattastvaṃ niyataṃ mokṣamāpsyasi  VamP 
na cet tatpāpaśīlo 'hamatyarthaṃ kṣutpipāsitaḥ 
ṣaṣṭhe kāle nṛśaṃsātmā bhakṣayiṣyāmi nirghṛṇaḥ  VamP 
pulastya uvāca 
evamukto munisutastena ghorema rakṣasā 
cintāmavāpa mahatīmaśaktastadudīraṇe  VamP 
sa vimṛśya ciraṃ vipraḥ śaraṇaṃ jātavedasam 
jagāma jñānadānāya saṃśayaṃ paramaṃ gataḥ  VamP 
yadi śuśruṣito vahnirguruśuśrūṣaṇādanu 
vratāni vā sucīrṇāni saptārciḥ pātu māṃ tataḥ  VamP 
na mātaraṃ na pitaraṃ gauraveṇa yathā gurum 
sarvadaivāvagacchāmi tathā māṃ pātu pāvakaḥ  VamP 
yathā guruṃ na manasā karmaṇā vacasāpi vā 
avajānāmyahaṃ tena pātu satyena pāvakaḥ  VamP 
ityevaṃ manasā satyān kurvataḥ śapathān punaḥ 
saptarciṣā samādiṣṭā prādurāsīt sarasvatī  VamP 
sā provāca dvijasutaṃ rākṣasagrahaṇākulam 
mā bhairdvijasutāhaṃ tvāṃ mokṣayiṣyāmi saṃkaṭāt  VamP 
yadasya rakṣasaḥ śreyo jihvāgre saṃsthitā tava 
tat sarvaṃ kathayiṣyāmi tato mokṣamavāpsyasi  VamP 
adṛśyā rakṣasā tena proktvetthaṃ sā sarasvatī 
adarśānaṃ gatā so 'pi dvijaḥ prāha niśācaram  VamP 
brāhmaṇa uvāca 
śruyatāṃ tava yacchreyastathānyeṣāṃ ca pāpinām 
samastapāpaśuddhyarthaṃ puṇyopacayadaṃ ca yat  VamP 
prātarutthāya japtavyaṃ madhyāhne 'hnakṣaye 'pi vā 
asaṃśayaṃ sadā japyo japatāṃ puṣṭiśāntidaḥ  VamP 
oṃ hariṃ kuṣṇaṃ hṛṣīkeśaṃ vāsudevaṃ janārdanam 
praṇato 'smi jagannāthaṃ sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu  VamP 
carācarasuruṃ nāthaṃ govindaṃ śeṣaśāyinam 
praṇato 'smi paraṃ devaṃ sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu  VamP 
śaṅkhinaṃ cakriṇaṃ śārṅgadhāriṇaṃ sragdharaṃ param 
praṇato 'smi patiṃ lakṣmyāḥ sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu  VamP 
dāmodaramudārākṣaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣamacyutam 
praṇato 'smi stutaṃ stutyaiḥ sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu  VamP 
nārāyaṇaṃ naraṃ śauriṃ mādhavaṃ madhusūdanam 
praṇato 'smi dharādhāraṃ sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu  VamP 
keśavaṃ candrasūryākṣaṃ kaṃsakeśiniṣūdanam 
praṇato 'smi mahābāhuṃ sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu  VamP 
śrīvatsavakṣasaṃ śrīśaṃ śrīdharaṃ śrīniketanam 
praṇato 'smi śriyaḥ kāntaṃ sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu  VamP 
yamīśaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ dhyāyanti yatayo 'kṣaram 
vāsudevamanirdeśyaṃ tamasmi śaraṇaṃ gataḥ  VamP 
samastālambanebhyo yaṃ vyāvṛttya manaso gatim 
dhyāyanti vāsudevākhyaṃ tamasmi śaraṇaṃ gataḥ  VamP 
sarvagaṃ sarvabhūtaṃ ca sarvasyādhāramīśvaram 
vāsudevaṃ paraṃ brahma tamasmi śaraṇaṃ gataḥ  VamP 
paramātmānamavyaktaṃ yaṃ prayānti sumedhasaḥ 
karmakṣaye 'kṣayaṃ devaṃ tamasmi śaraṇaṃ gataḥ  VamP 
puṇyapāpavinirmuktā yaṃ praviśya punarbhavam 
na yoginaḥ prāpnuvanti tamasmi śaraṇaṃ gataḥ  VamP 
brahma bhūtvā jagat sarvaṃ sadevāsuramānuṣam 
yaḥ sṛjatyacyuto devastamasmi śaraṇaṃ gataḥ  VamP 
brahmatve yasya vaktrebhyaścaturvedamayaṃ vapuḥ 
prabhuḥ purātano jajñe tamasmi śaraṇaṃ gataḥ  VamP 
brahmarūpadharaṃ devaṃ jagadyoni janārdanam 
sraṣṭṛtve saṃsthitaṃ sṛṣṭau praṇato 'smi sanātanam  VamP 
sraṣṭā bhūtvā sthito yogī sthitāvasurasūdanaḥ 
tamādipuruṣaṃ viṣṇuṃ pramato 'smi janārdanam  VamP 
dhṛtā mahī hatā daityāḥ paritrātāstathā surāḥ 
yena taṃ viṣṇumādyeśaṃ praṇato 'smi janārdanam  VamP 
yajñairyajanti yaṃ viprā yajñeśaṃ yajñabhāvanam 
taṃ yajñapuruṣaṃ viṣṇuṃ praṇato 'smi sanātanam  VamP 
pātālavīthībhūtānu tathā lokān nihanti yaḥ 
tamantapuruṣaṃ rudraṃ praṇato 'smi sanātanam  VamP 
saṃbhakṣayitvā sakalaṃ yathāsṛṣṭamidaṃ jagat 
yo vai nṛtyati rudrātmā praṇato 'smi janārdanam  VamP 
surāsurāḥ pitṛgaṇāḥ yakṣagandharvarākṣasāḥ 
saṃbhūtā yasya devasya sarvagaṃ taṃ namāmyaham  VamP 
samastadevāḥ sakalā manuṣyāṇāṃ ca jātayaḥ 
yasyāṃśabhūtā devasya sarvagaṃ taṃ nato 'smayaham  VamP 
vṛkṣagulmādayo yasya tathā paśumṛgādayaḥ 
ekāṃśabhūtā devasya sarvagaṃ taṃ namāmyaham  VamP 
yasmānnānyat paraṃ kiñcid yasmin sarvaṃ mahātmani 
yaḥ sarvamadhyago 'nantaḥ sarvagaṃ taṃ namāmyaham  VamP 
yathā sarveṣu bhūteṣu gūḍho 'gniriva dāruṣu 
viṣṇurevaṃ tathā pāpaṃ mamāśeṣaṃ praṇaśyatu  VamP 
yathā viṣṇumayaṃ sarvaṃ brahmadi sacarācaram 
yacca jñānaparicchedyaṃ pāpaṃ naśyatu me tathā  VamP 
śubhaśubhāni karmāṇi rajaḥsattvatamāṃsi ca 
anekajanmakarmotthaṃ pāpaṃ naśyatu me tathā  VamP 
yanniśāyāṃ ca yatprātaryanmadhyāhnāparāhṇayoḥ 
saṃdhyayośca kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ karmaṇā manasā girā  VamP 
yat tiṣṭhatā yad vrajatā yacca śayyāgatena me 
kṛtaṃ yadaśubhaṃ karma kāyena manasā girā  VamP 
ajñānato jñānato vā madāccalitamānasaiḥ 
tat kṣipraṃ vilayaṃ yātu vāsudevasya kīrtanāt  VamP 
paradāraparadravyavāñchādrohodbhavaṃ ca yat 
parapīḍodbhavāṃ nindāṃ kurvatā yanmahātmanām  VamP 
yacca bhojye tathā peye bhakṣye coṣye vilehane 
tad yātu vilayaṃ toye yathā lavaṇabhājanam  VamP 
yad bālye yacca kaumāre yat pāpaṃ yauvane mama 
vayaḥpariṇatau yacca yacca janmātare kṛtam  VamP 
tannārāyaṇa govinda harikṛṣṇeśa kīrtanāt 
prayātu vilayaṃ toye yathā lavaṇabhājanam  VamP 
viṣṇave vāsudevāya haraye keśavāya ca 
janārdanāya kṛṣṇāya namo bhūyo namo namaḥ  VamP 
bhaviṣyannarakaghnāya namaḥ kaṃsavighātine 
ariṣṭakeśicaṇūradevārikṣayiṇe namaḥ  VamP 
ko 'nyo balervañcayitā tvāmṛte vai bhaviṣyati 
ko 'nyo nāśayati balād darpaṃ haihayabhūpateḥ  VamP 
kaḥ kariṣyatyathānyo vai sāgare setubandhanam 
vadhiṣyati daśagrīvaṃ kaḥ sāmātyapuraḥsaram  VamP 
kastvāmṛte 'nyo nandasya gokule ratimeṣyati 
pralambapūtanādīnāṃ tvāmṛte madhusūdana 
nihantāpyathabā śāstā devadeva bhaviṣyati  VamP 
japannevaṃ naraḥ puṇyaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ dharmamuttamam 
iṣṭāniṣṭaprasaṃgebhyo jñānato 'jñānato 'pi vā  VamP 
kṛtaṃ tena tu yat pāpaṃ saptajanmāntarāṇi vai 
mahāpātakasaṃjñaṃ vā tathā caivopapātakam  VamP 
jajñādīni ca puṇyāni japahomavratāni ca 
nāśayed yogināṃ sarvamāmapātramivāmbhasi  VamP 
naraḥ saṃvatsaraṃ pūrṇaṃ tilapātrāṇi ṣoḍaśa 
ahanyahani yo dadyāt paṭhatyetacca tatsamam  VamP 
aviluptabrahmacaryaṃ saṃprāpya smaraṇaṃ hareḥ 
viṣṇulokamavāpnoti satyametanmayoditam  VamP 
yathaitat stayamuktaṃ me na hyalpamapi me mṛṣā 
rākṣasastrastasarvāṅgaṃ tathā māmeṣa muñcatu  VamP 
pulastya uvāca 
evamuccārite tena mukto viprastu rakṣasā 
akāmena dvijo bhūyastamāha rajanīcaram  VamP 
brahmaṇa uvāca 
etad bhadra mayā khyātaṃ tava pātakanāśanam 
viṣṇoḥ sārasvataṃ stotraṃ yajjagāda sarasvatī  VamP 
hutāśanena prahitā mama jihvāgrasaṃsthitā 
jagādainaṃ stavaṃ viṣṇoḥ sarveṣāṃ copaśāntidam  VamP 
anenaiva jagannāthaṃ tvamārādhaya kesavam 
tataḥ śāpāpanodaṃ tu stute lapsyasi keśave  VamP 
aharniśaṃ hṛṣīkeśaṃ stavenānena rākṣasa 
stuhi bhaktiṃ dṛḍhāṃ kṛtvā tataḥ pāpād vimokṣyase  VamP 
stuto hi sarvapāpāni nāśayiṣyatyasaṃśayam 
stuto hi bhaktyā nṝṇāṃ vai sarvapāpaharo hariḥ  VamP 
pulastya uvāca 
tataḥ praṇamya taṃ vipraṃ prasādya sa niśācaraḥ 
tadaiva tapase śrīmān śālagrāmamagād vaśī  VamP 
aharniśaṃ sa evainaṃ japan sārasvataṃ stavam 
devakriyāratirbhūtvā tapastepe niśācaraḥ  VamP 
samārādhya jagannāthaṃ sa tatra puraṣottamam 
sarvapāpavinirmukto viṣṇulokamavāptavān  VamP 
etat te kathitaṃ brahman viṣṇoḥ sārasvataṃ stavam 
vipravaktrasthayā samyaksarasvatyā samīritam  VamP 
ya etat paramaṃ stotraṃ vāsudevasya mānavaḥ 
paṭhaṣyati sa sarvebhyaḥ pāpebhyo mokṣamāpsyati  VamP 
iti śrīvāmanapurāṇe ekonaṣaṣṭitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
pulastya uvāca 
namaste 'stu jagannātha devadevaṃ namo 'stu te 
vāsudeva namaste 'stu bahurūpa namo 'stu te  VamP 
ekaśṛṅga namastubhyaṃ namastubhyaṃ vṛṣākape 
śrīnivāsa namaste 'stu namaste bhūtabhāvana  VamP 
viṣvaksena namastubhyaṃ nārāyaṇa namo 'stu te 
dhruvadhvaja namasto 'stu satyadhvaja namo 'stu te  VamP 
yajñadhvaja namastubhyaṃ dharmadhvaja namo 'stu te 
tāladhvaja namaste 'stu namaste garuhadhvaja  VamP 
vareṇya viṣṇo vaikuṇṭha namaste puruṣottama 
namo jayanta vijaya jayānanta parājita  VamP 
kṛtāvartada mahāvarta mahādeva namo 'stu te 
anādyādyanta madhyānta namaste padmajapriya  VamP 
purañjaya namastubhyaṃ śatruñjaya namo 'stu te 
śubhañjaya namaste 'stu namaste 'stu dhanañjaya  VamP 
sṛṣṭigarbha namastubhyaṃ śuciśravaḥ vṛthuśravaḥ 
namo hiraṇyagarbhāya padmagarbhāya te namaḥ  VamP 
namaḥ kamalanetrāya kālanetrāya te namaḥ 
kālanābha namastubhyaṃ mahānābha namo namaḥ  VamP 
vṛṣṭimūla mahāmūla mūlāvāsa namo 'stu te 
dharmāvāsa jalāvāsa śrīnivāsa namo 'stu te  VamP 
dharmādhyakṣa prajādhyakṣa lokādhyakṣa namo namaḥ 
senādhyakṣa namastubhyaṃ kālādhyakṣa namo namaḥ  VamP 
gadādhara śrutidhara cakradhārin śriyo dhara 
vanamālādhara hare namaste dharaṇīdhara  VamP 
ārciṣeṇa mahāsena namaste 'stu puruṣṭuta 
vahukalpa mahākalpa namaste kalpanāmukha  VamP 
sarvātman sarvaga vibho viriñce śveta keśava 
nīla rakta mahānīla aniruddha namo 'stu te  VamP 
dvādaśātmaka kālātman sāmātman paramātmaka 
vyomakātmaka subrahman bhūtātmaka namo 'stu te  VamP 
harikeśa mahākeśa guḍākeśa namo 'stu te 
muñjakeśa hṛṣīkeśa sarvanātha mano 'stu te  VamP 
sukṣma sthūla mahāsthūla mahāsūkṣma śubhaṅkara 
śvetapītāmbaradhara nīlavāsa namo 'stu te  VamP 
kuśeśaya namaste 'stu sīradhvaja najārdhana 
govinda prītikartā ca haṃsa pītāmbarapriya  VamP 
adhokṣaja namastubhyaṃ sīradhvaja janārdana 
vāmanāya namaste 'stu namaste madhusūdana  VamP 
sahasraśīrṣāya namo brahmaśīrṣāya te namaḥ 
namaḥ sahasranetrāya somasūryānalekṣama 
namaścātharvaśirase mahāśīrṣāya te namaḥ 
namaste dharmanetrāya mahānetrāya te namaḥ  VamP 
namaḥ sahasrapādāya sahasrabhujamanyave 
namo yajñavarāhāya mahārūpāya te namaḥ  VamP 
namaste viśvadevāya viśvātman viśvasaṃbhava 
viśvarūpa namaste 'stu tvatto viśvamabhūdidam  VamP 
nyagrodhastavaṃ mahāśākhastvaṃ mūlakusumārcitaḥ 
skandhapatrāṅkuralatāpallavāya namo 'stu te  VamP 
mūlaṃ te brāhmaṇā brahman skandhaste kṣatriyordiśaḥ 
nābhyā hyabhūdantarikṣaṃ śaśāṅko manasastava  VamP 
brāhmaṇāḥ sāgnayo vaktrāḥ derdaṇḍāḥ sāyudhā nṛpāḥ 
pārśvād viśaśceruyugājjātāḥ śūdrāśca pādataḥ  VamP 
netrād bhānurabhūt tubhyaṃ padbhyāṃ bhūḥ śrotrayordiśaḥ 
nābhyā hyabhūdantarikṣaṃ śaśāṅko manasastava  VamP 
prāṇād vāyuḥ samabhavat kāmād brahmā pitāmahaḥ 
krodhāt trinayano rudraḥ śīrṣṇoḥ dyauḥ samavartata  VamP 
indrāgnī vadanāt tubhyaṃ paśavo malasaṃbhavāḥ 
oṣadhyo romasaṃbhūtā virājastvaṃ namo 'stu te  VamP 
puṣpahāsa namaste 'stu mahāhāsa namo 'stu te 
oṅkārastvaṃ vaṣaṭkāro vauṣaṭ tvaṃ ca svadhā sudhā  VamP 
svāhākāra namastubhyaṃ hantakāra namo 'stu te 
sarvākāra nirākāra vedākāra namo 'stu te  VamP 
tvaṃ hi vedamayo devaḥ sarvadevamayastathā 
sarvatīrthamayaścaiva sarvayajñamayastathā  VamP 
namaste yajñapuruṣa yajñabhāgabhuje namaḥ 
namaḥ sahasradhārāya śatadhārāya te namaḥ  VamP 
bhīrbhuvaḥsvaḥsvarūpāya godāyāmṛtadāyine 
suvarṇabrahmadātre ca sarvadātre ca te namaḥ  VamP 
brahmeśāya namastubhyaṃ brahmāde brahmarūpadhṛk 
parabrahma namaste 'stu śabdabrahma namo 'stu te  VamP 
vidyāstvaṃ vedyarūpastvaṃ vedanīyastvameva ca 
buddhistvamapi bodhyaśca bodhastvaṃ ca namo 'stu te  VamP 
hotā homaśca havyaṃ ca hūyamānaścahavyāvāṭ 
pātā potā ca putaśca pāvanīyaśca oṃ namaḥ  VamP 
hantā ca hanyamānaś ca hrimāṇastvameva ca 
harttā netā ca nītiśca pūjyo 'gryo viśvadhāryasi  VamP 
sruksruvau paradhāmāsi kapālolūkhalo 'raṇiḥ 
yajñapātrāṇeyastvamekadhā bahudhā tridhā  VamP 
yajñastvaṃ yajamānastvamīḍyastvamasi yājakaḥ 
jñātā jñeyastathā jñānaṃ dhyeyo dhyātāsi ceśvara  VamP 
dhyānayogaśca yogī ca gatirmokṣo dhṛtiḥ sukham 
yogāṅgāni tvamīśānaḥ sarvagastvaṃ namo 'stu te  VamP 
brahma hotā tathodgātā sāma yūpo 'ta dakṣiṇā 
dīkṣā tvaṃ tvaṃ puroḍāśastvaṃ paśuḥ paśuvāhyasi  VamP 
guhyo dhātā ca paramaḥ śivo nārāyaṇastathā 
mahājano nirayanaḥ sahasrārkendurūpavān  VamP 
dvādaśāro 'tha ṣaṇṇābhistrivyūho dviyugastathā 
kālacakro bhavānīśo namaste puruṣottamaḥ  VamP 
parākramo vikramastvaṃ hayagrīvo harīśvaraḥ 
nareśvaro 'tha brahmeśaḥ sūryeśastvaṃ namo 'stu te  VamP 
aśvavaktro mahāmedhāḥ śaṃbhuḥ śakraḥ prabhañjanaḥ 
mitrāvaruṇamūrtistvamamūrtiranaghaḥ paraḥ  VamP 
prāgvaṃśakāyo bhūtādirmahābhūto 'cyuto dvijaḥ 
tvamūrdhvakarttā ūrdhvaś ca ūrdhvaretā namo 'stu te  VamP 
mahāpātakahā tvaṃ ca upapātakahā tathā 
anīśaḥ sarvapāpebhyastvāmahaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ  VamP 
ityetat paramaṃ stotraṃ sarvapāpapramocanam 
maheśvareṇa kathitaṃ vārāṇasyāṃ purā mune  VamP 
keśavasyāgrato gatvā snātvā tīrthe sitodake 
upaśāntastathā jāto rudraḥ pāpavaśāt tataḥ  VamP 
etat pavitraṃ tripuradhnabhāṣitaṃ paṭhan naro viṣṇuparo maharṣe 
vimuktapāpo hyupaśāntamūrti saṃpūjyate devavaraiḥ prasiddhaiḥ  VamP 
iti śrīvāmanapurāṇe ṣaṣṭhitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
pulastya uvāca 
dvitīyaṃ pāpaśamanaṃ stavaṃ vakṣyāmi te mune 
yena samyagadhītena pāpaṃ nāśaṃ tu gaccati  VamP 
matsyaṃ namasye deveśaṃ kūrmaṃ govindameva ca 
hayaśīrṣaṃ namaste 'haṃ bhavaṃ viṣṇuṃ trivikramam  VamP 
namasye mādhaveśānau hṛṣīkaśakumāriṇau 
nārāyaṇaṃ namasye 'haṃ namasye garuḍāsanam  VamP 
ūrdhvakeśaṃ nṛsihaṃ ca rupadhāraṃ kurudhvajam 
kāmapālamakhaṇḍaṃ ca namasye brāhmaṇapriyam  VamP 
ajitaṃ viśvakarmāṇaṃ puṇḍarīkaṃ dvijapriyam 
haṃsaṃ śaṃbhuṃ namasye ca brahmāṇaṃ saprajāpatim  VamP 
namasye śūlabāhuṃ ca devaṃ cakradharaṃ tathā 
śivaṃ viṣṇuṃ suvarṇākṣaṃ gopatiṃ pītavāsasam  VamP 
namasye ca gadāpāṇiṃ namasye ca kuśośayam 
ardhanārīśvaraṃ devaṃ namasye pāpanāśanam  VamP 
gopālaṃ ca saivakuṇṭhaṃ namasye cāparājitam 
namasye viśvarūpaṃ ca saugandhiṃ sarvadāśivam  VamP 
pāñcālikaṃ hayagrīvaṃ svayambhuvamamareśvaram 
namasye puṣkarākṣaṃ ca payogandhiṃ ca keśavam  VamP 
avimuktaṃ ca lolaṃ ca jyeṣṭheyaṃ madhyamaṃ tathā 
upaśāntaṃ tamasye 'haṃ mārkaṇḍeyaṃ sajambukam  VamP 
namasye padmakiraṇaṃ namasye vaḍavāmukham 
kārttikeyaṃ namasye 'haṃ bāhlīkaṃ śikhinaṃ tathā  VamP 
namasye sthāṇumanaghaṃ namasye vanamālinam 
namasye lāṅgalīśaṃ ca namasye 'haṃ śriyaḥ patim  VamP 
namasye ca trinayanaṃ namasye havyavāhanam 
namasye ca trisauvarṇaṃ namasye śaśibhūṣaṇam  VamP 
triṇāciketaṃ brahmeśaṃ namasye śaśibhūṣaṇam 
kapardinaṃ namasye ca sarvāmayavināśanam  VamP 
namasye śaśinaṃ sūryaṃ dhruvaṃ raudraṃ mahaujasam 
padmanābhaṃ hiraṇyākṣaṃ namasye skandamavyayam  VamP 
namasye bhīmahaṃsau ca namasye hāṭakeśvaram 
sadā haṃsaṃ namasye ca namasye prāmatarpaṇam  VamP 
namasye rukmakavacaṃ mahāyoginamīśvaram 
namasye śrīnivāsaṃ ca namasye puruṣottamam  VamP 
namasye ca caturbāhuṃ namasye vasudhādhipam 
vanaspatiṃ paśupatiṃ namasye prabhumavyayām  VamP 
śrīkaṇṭhaṃ vāsudevaṃ nīlakaṇṭhaṃ sadaṇḍinam 
namasye sarvamanaghaṃ gaurīśaṃ nakulīsvaram  VamP 
manoharaṃ kṛṣṇakeśaṃ namasye cakrapāṇinam 
yaśodharaṃ mahābāhuṃ namasye ca kuśapriyam  VamP 
bhūdharaṃ chāditagadaṃ sunetraṃ śūlaśaṅkhinam 
bhadrākṣaṃ vīrabhadraṃ ca namasye śaṅkukarṇikam  VamP 
vaṣadhvajaṃ maheśaṃ ca viśvāmitraṃ śaśiprabham 
upendra caiva govindaṃ namaste paṅkajapriyam  VamP 
sahasraśirsaṃ devaṃ namasye kundamālinam 
kālāgniṃ rudradeveśaṃ namasye kṛttivāsasam  VamP 
namasye chāgaleśaṃ ca namasye paṅkajāsanam 
sahasrākṣaṃ kokanadaṃ namasye hariśaṅkaram  VamP 
agastayaṃ garuḍaṃ viṣṇuṃ kapilaṃ brahmavāṅmayam 
sanātanaṃ ca brahmāṇaṃ namasye brahmatatparam  VamP 
apratarkyaṃ caturbāhuṃ sahasrāṃśuṃ tapomayam 
namasye dharmarājānaṃ devaṃ garuḍavāhanam  VamP 
sarvabūtagataṃ śāntaṃ nirmalaṃ sarvalakṣaṇam 
mahāyoginamavyaktaṃ namasye pāpanāśanam  VamP 
nirañjanaṃ nirākāraṃ nirguṇaṃ nirmalaṃ padam 
namasye pāpahantāraṃ śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇaṃ vraje  VamP 
etat pavitraṃ paramaṃ purāṇaṃ proktaṃ tvagastayena maharṣiṇā ca 
dhnyaṃ yaśasyaṃ bahupāpanāśanaṃ saṃkartanāt smāraṇāt saṃśravācca  VamP 
iti śrīvāmanapurāṇe ekaṣaṣṭitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
pulastya uvāca 
gate 'tha tīrthayātrāyāṃ prahlāde dānaveśvare 
kurukṣetraṃ samabhyāgād yaṣṭuṃ vairocano valiḥ  VamP 
tasmin mahādharmayute tīrthe brāhmaṇapuṅgavaḥ 
śukro dvijātipravarānāmantrayat bhārgavān  VamP 
bhṛgūnāmantryamāṇān vai śrutvātreyāḥ sagautamāḥ 
kauśikāṅgirasaścaiva tatyajuḥ kurujāṅgalān  VamP 
uttarāśāṃ prajagmuste nadīmanu śatadrukām 
śātadrave jale snātvā vipāśāṃ prayayustataḥ  VamP 
vijñāya tatrāpyaratiṃ snātvār'cya pitṛdevatāḥ 
prajagmuḥ kiraṇāṃ puṇyāṃ dineśakiraṇacyutām  VamP 
tasyāṃ snātvār'cya deverṣe sarva eva maharṣayaḥ 
airāvatīṃ supuṇyodāṃ snātvā jagmuratheśvarīm  VamP 
devikāyā jale snātvā payoṣṇyāṃ caiva tāpasāḥ 
avatīrṇā mune snātumātreyādyāḥ śubhāṃ nadīm  VamP 
tato nimagnā dadṛśuḥ pratibimbamathātmanaḥ 
antarjale dvijaśreṣṭha mahadāścaryakārakam  VamP 
unmajjane ca dadṛśuḥ punarvismitamānasāḥ 
tataḥ snātvā samuttīrṇā ṛṣayaḥ sarva eva hi  VamP 
jagamustato 'pi te brahman kathayantaḥ parasparam 
cintayantaśca satataṃ kimetaditi vismitāḥ  VamP 
tato dūrādapaśyanta vanaṣaṇḍaṃ suvistṛtam 
vanaṃ haragalaśyāmaṃ khagadhvaninināditam  VamP 
atituṅgatayā vayoma āvṛṇvānaṃ nagottamam 
vistṛtābhirjaṭābhistu antarbhūmiñca nārada  VamP 
kānanaṃ puṣpitairvṛkṣairatibhāti samantataḥ 
daśārddhavarṇaiḥ sukhadairnabhastārāgaṇairiva  VamP

manyamānā gṛhadvāri ṣaṣṭhe 'hani samutsṛjat  VamP

svaṃ śiśuṃ kṛśamādāya sūrpākṣī nāma nāmataḥ  VamP 
tatrotsṛjya svaputraṃ sā jagrāha dvijanandanam 
tamādāya jagāmātha bhoktuṃ śālodare girau  VamP 
tatastāmāgatāṃ vīkṣya tasyā bhartā ghaṭodaraḥ 
netrahīnaḥ pratyuvāca kimānītastvayā priye  VamP 
sābravīt rākṣasapate mayā sthāpya nijaṃ śiśum 
kośakāradvijagṛhe tasyānītaḥ prabho sutaḥ  VamP 
sa prāha na tvayā bhadre bhadramācaritaṃ tviti 
mahājñānī dvijendro 'sau tataḥ śapsyati kopitaḥ  VamP 
tasmācchīghramimaṃ tyaktvā manujaṃ ghorarupiṇam 
anyasya kasyacit putraṃ śīghramānaya sundari  VamP 
ityevamuktā sā raudrā rākṣasī kāmacāriṇī 
samājagāma tvaritā samutpatya vihāyasam  VamP 
sa cāpi rākṣasasuto nisṛṣṭo gṛhabāhyataḥ 
ruroda susvaraṃ brahman prakṣipyāṅguṣṭhamānane  VamP 
sā kranditaṃ cirācchrutvā dharmiṣṭhā patimabravīt 
paśya svayaṃ muniśreṣṭha saśabdastanayastava  VamP 
trastā sā nirjagāmātha gṛhamadhyāt tapasvinī 
sa cāpi brāhmaṇaśreṣṭhaḥ samapaśyata taṃ śiśum  VamP 
varṇarūpādisaṃyuktaṃ yathā svatanayaṃ tathā 
tato vihasya provāca kośakāro nijāṃ priyām  VamP 
etenāviśya dharmiṣṭhe bhāvyaṃ bhūtena sāmpratam 
ko 'pyaṭasmākaṃ chalayituṃ surūpī bhuvi saṃsthitaḥ  VamP 
ityuktvā vacanaṃ mantrī mantraistaṃ rākṣasātmajam 
babandhollikhya vasudhāṃ sakuśenātha pāṇinā  VamP 
etasminnantare prāptā sūrpākṣī viprabālakam 
antardhānagatā bhūmau cikṣepa gṛhadūrataḥ  VamP 
taṃ kṣiptamātraṃ jagrāha kośakāraḥ svakaṃ sutam 
sā cābhyetya grahītuṃ svaṃ nāśakad rākṣasī sutam  VamP 
itaścetaśca vibhraṣṭā sā bhartāramupāgamat 
kathayāmāsā yad vṛttaṃ svadvijātmajahīriṇam  VamP 
evaṃ gatāyaṃ rākṣasyāṃ brāhmaṇena mahātmanā 
sa rābhasaśiśurbrahman bhāryāyai viniveditaḥ  VamP 
sa cātmatanayaḥ pitrā kapilāyāḥ savatsayāḥ 
dadhnā saṃyojito 'tyarthaṃ kṣīreṇekṣurasena ca  VamP 
dvāveva vardhitau bālau saṃjātau saptavārṣikau 
pitrā ca kṛtanāmānau niśākaradivākarau  VamP 
naiśācarirdivākīrtirniśākīrtiḥ svaputrakaḥ 
tayoścakāra vipro 'sau vratabandhakriyāṃ kramāt  VamP 
vratabandhe kṛte vedaṃ papāṭhāsau divākaraḥ 
niśākaro jaḍatayā na papāṭheti naḥ śrutam  VamP 
taṃ bāndhavāśca pitarau mātā bhrātā gurustathā 
paryanindaṃstathā ye ca janā malayavāsinaḥ  VamP 
tataḥ sa pitrā kruddhena kṣiptaḥ kūpe nirūdake 
mahāśilāṃ copari vai pidhānamavaropayat  VamP 
evaṃ kṣiptastadā kūpe samatīteṣu bhārgava 
tasya mātāgamat kūpaṃ tamandhaṃ śilayācitam  VamP 
tato daśasu varṣeṣu samatīteṣu bhārgava 
tasya mātāgamat kūpaṃ tamandhaṃ śilayācitam  VamP 
sā dṛṣṭāvā nicitaṃ kūpaṃ śilayā girikalpayā 
uccaiḥ provāca keneyaṃ kūpopari śilā kṛtā  VamP 
kūpāntasthaḥ sa tāṃ vāṇīṃ śrutvā māturniśākaraḥ 
prāha pradattā pitrā me kūpopari śilā tviyam  VamP 
sātibhītābravīt ko 'si kūpāntastho 'dbhutasvaraḥ 
so 'pyāha tava putro 'smi niśākareti viśrutaḥ  VamP 
sābravīt tanayo mahyaṃ nāmnā khyāto divākaraḥ 
niśākareti nāmnāho na kaścit tanayo 'sti me  VamP 
sa cāha pūrvacaritaṃ māturniravaśeṣataḥ 
sā śrutvā tāṃ śilāṃsubhraḥ samutkṣipyāntayo 'śripat  VamP 
sottīrya kūpāt bhagavan mātuḥ pādāvavandata 
sā svānurūpaṃ tanayaṃ dṛṣṭvā svasutasya ca  VamP 
tatastamādāya sutaṃ dharmiṣṭhā patimetya ca 
kathayāmāsa tatsarvaṃ ceṣṭitaṃ svasutasya ca  VamP 
tatonvapṛcchad vipro 'sau kimidaṃ tāta kāraṇam 
noktavān yadbhavān pūrvaṃ mahatkautūhalaṃ mama  VamP 
tacchrutvā vacanaṃ dhīmān kośakāraṃ dvijottamam 
prāha putro 'dbhutaṃ vākyaṃ mātaraṃ pitaraṃ tathā  VamP 
śrūyatāṃ kāraṇaṃ tāta yena mūkatvamāśritam 
mayā jaḍatvamanagha tathāndhatvaṃ svacakṣuṣaḥ  VamP 
pūrvamāsamahaṃ vipra kule vṛndārakasya tu 
vṛṣākapeśca tanayo mālāgarbhasamudbhavaḥ  VamP 
tataḥ pitā pāṭhayanmāṃ śāstraṃ dharmārthakāmadam 
mokṣaśāstraṃ paraṃ tāta setihāsaśrutiṃ tathā  VamP 
so 'haṃ tāta mahājñānī parāvaraviśāradaḥ 
jāto madāndhastenāhaṃ duṣkarmābhirato 'bhavam  VamP 
madāt samabhavallebhastena naṣṭā pragalbhatā 
viveko nāśamagamat mūrkhabhāvamupāgataḥ  VamP 
mūḍha bhāvatayā cātha jātaḥ pāparato 'smbhaham 
paradāraparārtheṣu matirme ca sadābhavat  VamP 
paradārābhimarśitvāt parārthaharaṇādapi 
mṛto 'smyudbndhanenāhaṃ narakaṃ rauravaṃ gataḥ  VamP 
tasmād varṣasahasrānte bhuktaśiṣṭe tadāgasi 
araṇye mṛgahā pāpaḥ saṃjāto 'haṃ mṛgādhipaḥ  VamP 
vyāghratve saṃsthitastāta baddhaḥ pañjaragaḥ kṛtaḥ 
narādhipena vibhunā nītaśca nagaraṃ nijam  VamP 
baddhasya piñjarasthasya vyāghratve 'dhiṣṭhitasya ha 
dharmārthakāmaśāstrāṇi pratyabhāsanta sarvaśaḥ  VamP 
tato nṛpatiśārdūlo gadāpāṇiḥ kadācana 
ekavastraparīdhāno nagarānniryayau bahiḥ  VamP 
tasya bhāryā jitā nāma rūpeṇāpratimā bhuvi 
sā nirgate tu ramaṇe mamāntikamupāgatā  VamP 
tāṃ dṛṣṭvā vavṛdhe mahyaṃ pūrvābhyāsānmanobhavaḥ 
yathaiva dharmaśāstrāṇi tathāhamavadaṃ ca tām  VamP 
rājaputri sukalyāṇi navayauvanaśālini 
cittaṃ harasi me bhīru kokilā dhvaninā yathā  VamP 
sā madvacanamākarṇya provāca tanumadhyamā 
kathamevāvayorvyāghra ratiyogamupeṣyati  VamP 
tato 'hamabruvaṃ tāta rājaputrīṃ sumadhyamām 
dvāramudghāṭayasvādya nirgamiṣyāmi satvaram  VamP 
sāpyayabravīd divā vyāghra loko 'yaṃ paripaśyati 
rātrāvudghāṭayiṣyāma tato raṃsyāva svecchayā  VamP 
tāmevāhamavocaṃ vai kālakṣepe 'hamakṣamaḥ 
tasmādudghāṭaya dvāraṃ māṃ bandhācca vimocaya  VamP 
tataḥ sā pīvaraśreṇī dvāramudghāṭayanmune 
udghāṭite tato dvāre nirgato 'haṃ bahiḥ śraṇāt  VamP 
pāśāni nigaḍādīni chinnāni hi balānmayā 
sā gṛhītā ca nṛpaterbhāryā ramitumicchatā  VamP 
tato dṛṣṭo 'smi nṛpaterbhṛtyairatulavikramaiḥ 
śastrahastaiḥ sarvataśca tairahaṃ pariveṣṭitaḥ  VamP 
mahāpāśaiḥ śṛṅkhalābhiḥ samāhatya ca mudgaraiḥ 
vadhyamāno 'bruvamahaṃ mā mā hiṃsadhvamākulāḥ  VamP 
te madvacanamākarṇya matvaiva rajanīcaram 
dṛḍhaṃ vṛkṣe samudbdhya ghātayanta tapodhana  VamP 
bhayo gataśca narakaṃ paradāraniṣevaṇāt 
mukto varṣasahasrānte jāto 'haṃ śvetagardabhaḥ  VamP 
brāhmaṇasyāgniveśyasya gehe bahukalatriṇaḥ 
tatrāpi sarvavijñānaṃ pratyabhāsat tato mama  VamP 
upavanāhyaḥ kṛtaścāsmi dvijayoṣidbhirādarāt 
ekadā navarāṣṭrīyā bhāryā tasyāgrajanmanaḥ  VamP 
vimatirnāmataḥ khyātā gantumaicchad gṛhaṃ pituḥ 
tāmuvāca patirgaccha āruhyaṃ śvetagardabham  VamP 
māsenāgamanaṃ kāryaṃ na stheyaṃ paratastataḥ 
ityevamuktā sā bhartrā tanvī māmadhiruhya ca  VamP 
bandhanādavamucyātha jagāma tvaritā mune 
tator'dhapathi sā tanvī matpṛṣṭhādavaruhya vai  VamP 
avatīrṇā nadīṃ snātuṃ svarūpā cārdravāsasā 
sāṅgopāṅgāṃ rūpavatīṃ dṛṣṭvā tāmahamādravam  VamP 
mayā cābhidrutā tūrṇaṃ patitā pṛthivītale 
tasyāmupari bho tāta patito 'haṃ bhṛśāturaḥ  VamP 
hṛṣṭo bhartrānusṛṣṭena nṛṇā tadanusāriṇā 
protkṣipya yaṣṭiṃ māṃ brahman samādhāvat tvarānvitaḥ  VamP 
tad bhayāt tāṃ parityajya pradruto dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ 
tato 'bhidravatastūrṇa khalīnarasanā mune  VamP 
mamāsaktā vaṃśagulme durmokṣe prāṇanāśane 
tatrāsaktasya ṣaḍrātrānmamābhūjjīvitakṣayaḥ  VamP 
gato 'smi narakaṃ bhūyastasmānmukto 'bhavaṃ śukaḥ 
mahāraṇye tathā baddhaḥ śabareṇa durātmanā  VamP 
pañjare kṣipya vikrīto vaṇikputrāya śāline 
tenāpyantaḥ puravare yuvatīnāṃ samīpataḥ  VamP 
śabdaśāstravidityeva doṣaghnaścetyavasthitaḥ 
tatrāsatastaruṇyastā odanāmbuphalādibhiḥ  VamP 
bhakṣyaiśca dāḍimaphalaiḥ puṣṇantyaharahaḥ pitaḥ 
kadācit padmapatrākṣī śyāmā pīnapayodharā  VamP 
suśroṇī tanumadhyā ca vaṇikputrapriyā śubhā 
nāmnā candrāvalī nāma samudghāṭyātha pañjaram  VamP 
māṃ jagrāha sucārvaṅgī karābhyāṃ cāruhāsinī 
cakāropari pīnābhyāṃ karābhyāṃ cāruhāsinī 
cakāropari pīnābhyāṃ stanābhyāṃ sā hi māṃ tataḥ  VamP 
tato 'haṃ kṛtavān bhāvaṃ tasyāṃ vilasituṃ plavan 
tato 'nuplapatastatra hāre markaṭabandhanam  VamP 
baddho 'haṃ pāpasaṃyukto mṛśca tadanantaram 
bhūyo 'pi narakaṃ ghoraṃ prapanno 'smi sudurmatiḥ  VamP 
tasmāccāhaṃ vṛṣatvaṃ vai gataścāṇḍālapakvaṇe 
sa caikadā māṃ śakaṭe niyojya svāṃ vilāsinīm  VamP 
samāropya mahātejā gantuṃ kṛtamatirvanam 
tato 'grataḥ sa caṇḍālo gatastvevāsya pṛṣṭhataḥ  VamP 
gāyantī yāti tacchrutvā jāto 'haṃ vyathitendriyaḥ 
pṛṣṭhastu samālokya viparyastastathotplutaḥ  VamP 
patito bhūmimagamam tadakṣe kṣaṇavikramāt 
yoktre subaddha evāsmi pañcatvamagamaṃ tataḥ  VamP 
bhūyo nimagno narake daśavarṣaśatānyapi 
atastava gṛhe jātastvahaṃ jātimanusmaran  VamP 
tāvantyevādya janmāni smarāmi cānupūrvaśaḥ 
pūrvābhyāsācca śāstrāṇi bandhanaṃ cāgataṃ mama  VamP 
tadahaṃ jātavijñāno nācariṣye kathañcana 
pāpāni ghorarūpāṇi manasā karmaṇā girā  VamP 
śubhaṃ vāpyaśubhaṃ vāpi svādhyāyaṃ śāstrajīvikā 
bandhanaṃ vā vadho vāpi pūrvābhyāsena jāyate  VamP 
jātiṃ yadā paurvikīṃ tu smarate tāta mānavaḥ 
tadā sa tebhyaḥ pāpebhyo śubhavardhanāya pāpakṣayāyātha mune hyaraṇyam 
bhavān divākīrtimimaṃ suputraṃ gārhasthyadharme viniyojayasva  VamP 
tasmād gamiṣye śubhavardhanāya pāpakṣayāyātha mune hyaraṇyam 
bhavān divākīrtimimaṃ suputraṃ gārhasthyadharme viniyojayasva  VamP 
baliruvāca 
ityevamuktvā sa niśākarastadā praṇamya mātāpitarau maharṣe 
jagāma puṇyaṃ sadanaṃ murāreḥ khyātaṃ badaryāśramamādyamīḍyam  VamP 
evaṃ purābhyāsaratasya puṃso bhavanti dānādhyayanādikāni 
tasmācca pūrvaṃ dvijavarya vai mayā abhyastamāsīnnanu te bravīmi  VamP 
dānaṃ tapo vādhyayanaṃ maharṣe steyaṃ mahāpātakamagnidāham 
jñānāni caivābyasaṃtāṃ hi pūrvaṃ bhavanti dharmārthaśāṃsi nātha  VamP 
pulastya uvāca 
ityevamuktvā balavān sa śukraṃ daityeśvaraḥ svaḥ gurumīśitāram 
dhyāyaṃstadāste madhukaiṭabhaghnaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ cakragadāsipāṇim  VamP 
iti śrīvāmanapurāṇe catuḥṣaṣṭitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
pulastya uvāca 
etasminnantare prāpto bhagavān vāmanākṛtiḥ 
jajñavāṭamupāgam uccairvacanamabravīt  VamP 
oṅkārapūrvāḥ śrutayo makhe 'smin tiṣṭhanti rūpeṇa tapodhanānām 
yajño 'śvamedhaḥ pravaraḥ kratūnāṃ mukhyastathā satriṣu daityanāthaḥ  VamP 
itthaṃ vacanamākarṇya dānavādhipatirvaśī 
sārghapātraḥ samabhyāgādyatra devaḥ sthito 'bhavat  VamP 
tator'cya devadeveśamarcyamarghādināsuraḥ 
bharadvājarṣiṇā sārdhaṃ yajñavāṭaṃ praveśayat  VamP 
praviṣṭamātraṃ deveśaṃ pratipūjya vadhānataḥ 
provāca bhagavan brūhi kiṃ dadmi tava mānada  VamP 
tato 'bravīt suraśreṣṭho daityarājānamavyayaḥ 
vihasya suciraṃ kālaṃ bharadvājamavekṣya ca  VamP 
gurormadīyasya gurustasyāstyagniparigrahaḥ 
na sa dhārayate bhūmyāṃ pārakyāṃ jātavedasam  VamP 
tadarthamabhiyāc'haṃ mama dānavapārthiva 
maccharīrapramāṇena dehi rājan padatrayam  VamP 
surārervacanaṃ śrutvā balirbhāryāmavekṣya ca 
bāṇaṃ ca tanayaṃ vīkṣya idaṃ vacanamabravīt  VamP 
na kevalaṃ pramāṇena vāmano 'yaṃ laghuḥ priye 
yena kramatrayaṃ maurkhyād yācate buddhito 'pi ca  VamP 
prayo vidhātālpadhiyāṃ narāṇāṃ bahiṣkṛtānāṃ ca mahānubhāgyaiḥ 
dhanādikaṃ bhūri na vai dadāti yatheha viṣṇorna bahuprayāsaḥ  VamP 
na dadāti vidhistasya yasya bhāgyaviparyayaḥ 
mayi dātari yaścāyamadya yācet padatrayam  VamP 
ityevamuktvā vacanaṃ mahātmā bhūyo 'pyuvācātha hariṃ danūjaḥ 
yācasva viṣṇo gajavājibhūmiṃ dāsīhiraṇyaṃ yadabhīpsitaṃ ca  VamP 
bhavān yācayitā viṣṇo ahaṃ dātā jagatpatiḥ 
dāturyācayiturlajjā kathaṃ na syāt padatraye  VamP 
rasātalaṃ vā vṛthivīṃ bhuvaṃ nākamathāpi vā 
etabhyaḥ katamaṃ dadyāṃ sthānaṃ yācasva vāmana  VamP 
vāmana uvāca 
gajāśvabhūhiraṇyādi tadarthibhyaḥ pradīyatām 
etāvatā tvahaṃ cārthī dehi rājan padatrayam  VamP 
ityevamukte vacane vāmanena mahāsuraḥ 
balirbhṛṅgāramādāya dadau viṣṇoḥ kramatrayam  VamP 
pāṇau tu patite toye divyaṃ rūpaṃ cakāra ha 
trailokyakramaṇārthāya bahurūpaṃ jaganmayam  VamP 
padbhyāṃ bhūmistathā jaṅghe nabhastrailokyavanditaḥ 
satyaṃ tapo jānuyugme ūrubhyāṃ merumandarau  VamP 
viśvedevā kaṭībhāge maruto vastiśīrṣagāḥ 
liṅge sthito manmathaśca vṛṣaṇābhyāṃ prajāpatiḥ  VamP 
kukṣibhyāmarṇavāḥ sapta jaṭhare bhuvanāni ca 
valiṣu triṣu nadyaśca yajñāstu jaṭhare sthitāḥ  VamP 
iṣṭāpūrtādayaḥ sarvāḥ kriyāstatra tu saṃsthitāḥ 
pṛṣṭhasthā vasavo devāḥ skandhau rudrairadhiṣaṭhitau  VamP 
bāhavaśca diśaḥ sarvā vasavo 'ṣṭau kare smṛtāḥ 
hṛdaye saṃsthito brahmā kuliśo hṛdayāsthiṣu  VamP 
śrīsamudrā uromadhye candramā manasi sthitaḥ 
grīvāditirdevamātā vidyāstadvalayasthitāḥ  VamP 
mukhe tu sāgnayo viprāḥ saṃskārā daśanacchadāḥ 
dharmakāmārthamokṣīyāḥ śāstraḥ śaucasamanvitāḥ  VamP 
lakṣmyā saha lalāṭasthāḥ śravaṇābhyāmathāśvinau 
śvāsastho mātariśvā ca marutaḥ sarvasaṃdhiṣu  VamP 
sarvasūktāni daśānā jihvā devī sarasvatī 
candrādityau ca nayane pakṣmasthāḥ kṛttikādayaḥ  VamP 
śikhāyāṃ devadevasya dhruvo rājā nyaṣīdata 
tārakā romakūpebhyo romāṇi ca maharṣayaḥ  VamP 
guṇaiḥ sarvamayo bhūtvā bhagavān bhūtabhāvanaḥ 
krameṇaikena jagatīṃ jahāra sacarācarām  VamP 
bhūmiṃ vikramamāṇasya mahārūpasya tasya vai 
dakṣiṇo 'bhūt stanaścandraḥ sūryo 'bhūdatha cottaraḥ 
nakṣaścākramato nābhiṃ sūryendū savyadakṣiṇau  VamP 
dvitīyena krameṇātha svarmaharjanatāpasāḥ 
krāntārdhārdhena vairājaṃ madhyenāpūryatāmbaram  VamP 
tataḥ pratāpinā brahman bṛhadviṣṇvaṅghriṇāmbare 
brahmāṇḍodaramāhatya nirālokaṃ jagāma ha  VamP 
viśvāṅghriṇā prasaratā kaṭāho bhedito balān 
kuṭilā viṣṇupāde tu sametya kuṭilā tataḥ  VamP 
tasyā viṣṇupadītyevaṃ nāmākhyātamabhūnmune 
tathā suranadītyevaṃ tāmasevanta tāpasāḥ 
bhagavānapyasaṃpūrṇe tṛtīye tu krame vibhuḥ  VamP 
samabhyetya baliṃ prāha īṣat prasphuritādharaḥ 
ṛmād bhavati daityendra bandhanaṃ ghoradarśanam 
tvaṃ pūraya padaṃ tanme no ced bandhaṃ pratīccha bhoḥ  VamP 
tanmurārivacaḥ śrutvā vihasyātha baleḥ sutaḥ 
bāṇaḥ prāhāmarapatiṃ vacanaṃ hetusaṃyutam  VamP 
bāṇa uvāca 
kṛtvā mahīmalpatarāṃ jagatpate svāyaṃbhuvādibhuvanāni vai ṣaṭ 
kathaṃ baliṃ prārthayase suvistṛtāṃ yāṃ prāgbhavān no vipulāmathākarot  VamP 
vibho sahī yāvatīyaṃ tvayādya sṛṣṭacā sametā bhuvanāntarālaiḥ

viṣvaksena nārāyaṇa

 tenamasta  
oṃ namaste viśvadeveśa viśvabhūḥ viśvātmaka viśvarūpa viśvasaṃbhava tvatto viśvāmidamabhavad
brāhmaṇāstvanmukhebhyo 'bhavan kṣatriyā doḥsaṃbhūtāḥ ūruyugmād viso 'bhavan śūdrāścaraṇakamalebhyaḥ 
nābhyā bhavato 'ntarikṣamajāyata indrāgnīvaktrato netrād bhānurabhūnmanasaḥ śaśāṅkaḥ
ahaṃ prasādajastava krodhāt tryambakaḥ prāṇājjāto bhavato mātariśvā śiraso dyaurajāyata

 svarge sahasraṃ sa tu yojanānāṃ viṣṇoḥ pramāṇena hi vāmano 'bhūt tatrāsya śakraḥ pracakāra pūjāṃ svayaṃbhuvastulyaguṇāṃ maharṣe  VamP

areṣu saṃsthitā devāḥ sendrāḥ sārkāḥ sapāvakāḥ

tvannāmakīrtanāc cakra duritaṃ yātu saṃkṣayam  VamP 
ityevamuktvā matimān samabhyarcyātha bhaktitaḥ

prahlāda uvāca 
sādhu dānavaśārdūla yatte jātā matistviyam 
pravakṣyāmi hitaṃ te 'dya tathāneyeṣāṃ hitaṃ bale  VamP 
bhavajaladhigatānāṃ dvāndvavātāhatānāṃ sutaduhitṛkalatratrāṇabhārārditānām

ye saṃśritā harimanantamanādimadhyaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ suraguruṃ śubhadaṃ vareṇyam 
śuddhaṃ khagendragamanaṃ kamalālayeśaṃ te dharmarājakaraṇaṃ na viśanti dhīrāḥ 
 svapuruṣamabhivīkṣya pāśahastaṃ vadati yamaḥ kila tasya karṇamūle 
parihara madhusūdanaprannān prabhurahamanyanṛṇāṃ na vaiṣṇavānām  VamP 
tathānyaduktaṃ narasattamena ikṣvākuṇā bhaktiyutena nūnam 
ye viṣṇubhaktāḥ puruṣāḥ pṛthivyāṃ yamasya te nirviṣayā bhavanti  VamP 
sā jihvā yā hariṃ stauti taccittaṃ yattadarpitam 
tāveva kevalaṃ śalāghyau yau tatpūjākarau karau  VamP 
nūnaṃ na tau karau proktau vṛkṣaśākhāgrapallavau 
na yau pūjituṃ śaktau haripādāmbujadvayam  VamP 
nūnaṃ tatkaṇṭhaśālūkamathavā pratijihvakā 
rogovānyo na sā jihvā yā na vakti harerguṇān  VamP 
śocanīyaḥ sa bandhūnāṃ jīvannapi mṛto naraḥ 
yaḥ pādapaṅkajaṃ viṣṇorna pūjayati bhaktitaḥ  VamP 
ye narā vāsudevasya satataṃ pūjane ratāḥ 
mṛtā api na śocyāste satyaṃ satyaṃ mayoditam  VamP 
śārīraṃ mānasaṃ vāgjaṃ mūrtāmūrtaṃ carācaram 
dṛśyaṃ spṛsyamadṛśyañca tatsarvaṃ keśavātmakam  VamP 
yenārcito hi bhagavān caturdhā vai trivikramaḥ 
tenārcitā na saṃdeho lokāḥ sāmaradānavāḥ  VamP 
yatā ratnāni jaladherasaṃkhyeyāni putraka 
tathā guṇā hi devasya tvasaṃkhyātāstu cakriṇaḥ  VamP 
ye śaṅkhacakrābjakaraṃ saśārṅgiṇaṃ khagendraketuṃ varadaṃ śriyaḥ patim 
samāśrayante bhavabhītināśanaṃ saṃsāragarte na patanti te punaḥ  VamP 
yeṣāṃ manasi govindo nivāsī satataṃ bale 
na te paribhavaṃ yānti na mṛtyorudvijanti ca  VamP 
devaṃ sārṅgadharaṃ viṣṇuṃ ye prapannāḥ parāyaṇam 
na teṣāṃ yamasālokyaṃ na ca te narakaukasaḥ  VamP 
na tāṃ gatiṃ prāpnuvanti śrutiśāstraviśāradāḥ 
viprā dānavaśārdūla viṣṇubhaktā vrajanti yām  VamP 
yā gatirdaityaśārdūla hatānāṃ tu mahāhave 
tato 'dikāṃ gatiṃ yānti viṣṇubhaktā narottamāḥ  VamP 
yā gatirdharmaśīlānāṃ sāttvikānāṃ mahātmanām 
sā gatirgaditā daitya bhagavatsevināmapi  VamP 
sarvāvāsaṃ vāsudevaṃ sūkṣmamavyaktavigraham 
praviśanti mahātmānaṃ tadbhaktā nānyacetasaḥ  VamP 
ananyamanaso bhaktyā ye namasyanti keśavam 
śucayaste mahātmānastīrthabhūtā bhavanti te  VamP 
gacchan tiṣṭhan svapan jāgrat pibannaścannabhīkṣṇaśaḥ 
dhyāyan nārāyaṇaṃ yastu na tato 'nyo 'sti puṇyabhāk 
vaikuṇṭhaṃ khaḍgaparaśuṃ bhavabandhasamucchidam  VamP 
praṇipatya yathānyāyaṃ saṃsāre na punarbhavet 
kṣetreṣu vasate nityaṃ krīḍannāste 'mitadyutiḥ  VamP 
āsīnaḥ sarvadeheṣu karmabhirna sa badhyate 
yeṣāṃ viṣṇuḥ priyontyante viṣṇoḥ satataṃ priyāḥ  VamP 
na te punaḥ sambhavanti tadbhaktāstatparāyaṇāḥ 
dhyāyed dāmodaraṃ yastu bhaktinamror'cayeta vā  VamP 
na sa saṃsārapaṅke 'smin majjate dānaveśvara 
kalyamutthāya ye bhaktyā smaranti madhusūdanam 
stuvantyapyabhiśṛṇvanti durgaṇyatitaranti te  VamP 
harivākyāmṛtaṃ pītvā vimalaiḥ śrotrabhājanaiḥ 
prahṛṣyati mano yeṣāṃ durgāṇyatitaranti te  VamP 
yeṣāṃ cakragadāpāṇau bhaktiravyabhicāriṇī 
te yānti niyataṃ sthānaṃ yatra yogeśvaro hariḥ  VamP 
viṣṇukarmaprasaktānāṃ bhaktānāṃ yā parā gatiḥ 
sā tu janmasahasreṇa na tapobhiravāpyate  VamP 
kiṃ japyaistasya mantrairvā kiṃ tapobhiḥ kimāśramaiḥ 
yasya nāsti parā bhaktiḥ satataṃ madhusūdane  VamP 
vṛthā yajñā vṛtā vedā vṛthā dānaṃ vṛthā śrutam 
vṛthā tapaśca kīrtiśca yo dveṣṭi madhusūdanam  VamP 
kiṃ tasya bahurbharmantrairbhaktiryasya janārdane 
namo nārāyaṇāyeti mantraḥ sarvārthasādhakaḥ  VamP 
viṣṇureva gatiryoṣāṃ kutasteṣāṃ parājayaḥ 
yeṣāmindīvaraśyāmo hṛdayastho janārdanaḥ  VamP 
sarvamaṅgalamāṅgalyaṃ vareṇyaṃ varadaṃ prabhum 
nārāyaṇaṃ namaskṛtya sarvakarmāṇi kārayet  VamP 
viṣṭayo vyatipātāśca ye 'nye durnītisambhavāḥ 
te nāma smaraṇādviṣṇornāsaṃ yānti mahāsura  VamP 
tīrthakoṭisahasrāṇi tīrthakoṭiśatāni ca 
nārāyaṇapraṇāmasya kalāṃ nārhanti ṣoḍaśīm  VamP 
pṛthivyāṃ yāni tīrthāni puṇyānyāyatanāni ca 
tāni sarvāṇyavāpnoti viṣṇornāmānukīrtanāt  VamP 
prāpnuvanti na tāṃllokān vratino vā tapasvinaḥ 
prāpyante ye tu kṛṣṇasya namaskāraparairna raiḥ  VamP 
yo 'pyanyadevatābhakto mithyārcayati keśavam 
so'pi gacchati sādhūnāṃ sthānaṃ puṇyakṛtāṃ mahat  VamP 
sātatyena hṛṣīkeśaṃ pūjayitvā tu yatphalam 
sucīrṇatapasāṃ nṝṇāṃ tatā phalaṃ na kadācana  VamP 
trisandhyaṃ padmānābhaṃ tu ye smaranti sumedhasaḥ 
te labhantyupavāsasya phalaṃ nāsatyatra saṃśayaḥ  VamP 
satataṃ śāstradṛṣṭena karmaṇā harimarcaya 
tatprasādāt parāṃ siddhiṃ bale prāpsyasi śāśvatīm  VamP 
tanmanā bhava tadbhaktastadyājī taṃ namaskuru 
tamevāśritya deveśaṃ sukhaṃ prāpyasi putraka  VamP 
ādyaṃ hyanantamajaraṃ harimavyayaṃ ca ye vai smarantyaharaharnṛvarā bhuvisthāḥ 
sarvatragaṃ śubhadaṃ brahmamayaṃ purāṇam te yānti vaiṣṇavapadaṃ dhruvamakṣayañca  VamP 
ye mānavā vigatarāgaparāparajñā nārāyaṇaṃ suraguruṃ satataṃ smaranti 
te dhautapāṇḍurapuṭā iva rājahaṃsāḥ saṃsārasāgarajalasya taranti pāram  VamP 
dhyāyanti ye satatamacyutamīśitāraṃ niṣkalmaṣaṃ pravarapadmadalāyatākṣam 
dhyānena tena hatakilbaṣavedanāste mātuḥ payodhararasaṃ na punaḥ pibanti  VamP 
ye kīrtayanti varadaṃ varapadmanābhaṃ śaṅkhābjacakravaracāpagadāsihastam 
padmālayāvadanapaṅkajaṣaṭpadākhyaṃ nūnaṃ prayānti sadanaṃ madhughātinaste  VamP 
śṛṇvanti ye bhaktiparā manuṣyāḥ saṃkīrtyamānaṃ bhagavantamādyam 
te muktapāpāḥ sukhino bhavanti yathāmṛtaprāśanatarpitāstu  VamP 
tasmād dhyānaṃ smaraṇaṃ kīrtanaṃ vā nāmnāṃ śravaṇaṃ paṭhatāṃ sajjanānām 
kāryaṃ viṣṇoḥ śraddadhānairmanuṣyaiḥ pūjātulyaṃ tat praśaṃsanti devā  VamP 
bāhyaistathāntaḥkaraṇairaviklavairyo nārcayet keśavamīśitaram 
puṣpaiśca patrairjalapallavādibhirnūnaṃ sa muṣṭo vidhitaskareṇa  VamP 
iti śrīvāmanapurāṇe saptaṣaṣṭitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
baliruvāca 
bhavatā kathitaṃ sarvaṃ samārādhya janārdanam 
yā gatiḥ prāpyate loke tāṃ me vaktumihārhasi  VamP 
kenārcanena devasya prītiḥ samupajāyate 
kāni dānāni śastāni prīṇanāya jagadguroḥ  VamP 
upavāsādikaṃ kāryaṃ kasyāṃ tithyāṃ mahodayam 
kāni puṇyāni śastāni viṣṇostuṣṭipradāni vai  VamP 
yaccānyadapi karttavyaṃ hṛṣṭarūpairanālasaiḥ 
tadapyaśeṣaṃ daityendra mamākhyātumihārhasi  VamP 
prahlāda uvāca 
śraddadhānairbhaktiparairyānyuddiśya janārdanam 
bale dānāni dīyante tānūcurmunayo 'kṣayān  VamP 
tā eva tithayaḥ śastā yāsvabhyarcya jagatpatim 
taccittastanmayo bhūtvā upavāsī naro bhavet  VamP 
pūjiteṣu dvijendreṣu pūjitaḥ syājjanārdanaḥ 
etān dviṣanti ye mūḍhāste yānti narakaṃ dhruvam  VamP 
tānarcayennaro bhaktyā brāhmaṇān viṣṇutatparaḥ 
evamāha hariḥ pūrvaṃ brāhmaṇā māmakī tanuḥ  VamP 
brāhmaṇo nāvamantavyo budho vāpyabudho 'pi vā 
so 'pi divyā tanurviṣṇostasmāt tāmarcayennaraḥ  VamP 
tānyeva ca praśastāni kusumāni mahāsura 
yāni syurvarṇayuktāni rasagandhayutāni ca  VamP 
viśeṣataḥ pravakṣyāmi puṣpāṇi tithayastathā 
dānāni ca praśastāni mādhavaprīṇanāya tu  
 jātī śatāhvā sumanāḥ kundaṃ bahupuṭaṃ tathā 
bāṇañca campakāśokaṃ karavīraṃ ca yūthikā  VamP 
pāribhadraṃ pāṭalā ca bakulaṃ giriśālinī 
tilakaṃ ca japākusumaṃ pītakaṃ nāgaraṃ tvapi  VamP 
etāni hi praśastāni kusumānyacyutārcane 
surabhīṇi tathānyāni varjayitvā tu ketakīm  VamP 
bilvapatraṃ śamīpatraṃ patraṃ bhṛṅgamṛgāṅkayoḥ 
tamālāmalakīpatraṃ śastaṃ keśavapūjane  VamP 
yeṣāmapi hica puṣpāṇi praśastānyacyutārcane 
pallavānyapi teṣāṃ stuḥ patrāṇyarcāvidhau hareḥ 
 vīrudhāṃ ca pravālena barhiṣā cārcayettathā 
nānārūpaiścāmbubhavaiḥ kamalendīvarādibhiḥ  VamP 
pravālaiḥ śucibhiḥ ślakṣṇairjalaprakṣālitairbale 
vanaspatīnāmarcyeta tathā dūrvāgrapallavaiḥ  VamP 
candanenānulimpeta kuṅkumena prayatnanataḥ 
uśīrapadmakābhyāṃ ca tathā kālīyakādinā  VamP 
mahiṣākhyaṃ kaṇaṃ dāru sihlakaṃ sāgaruṃ sitā 
śaṅkhaṃ jātīphalaṃ śrīśe dhūpāni syuḥ priyāṇi vai  VamP 
haviṣā saṃskṛtā ye tu yavagodhūmaśālayaḥ 
tilamudgādayo māṣā vrīhayaśca priyā hareḥ  VamP 
godānāni pavitrāṇi bhūmidānāni cānagha 
vastrānnasvarṇadānāni prītaye madhughātinaḥ  VamP 
māghamāse tilā deyāstiladhenuśca dānava 
indhanādīni ca tathā mādhavaprīṇanāya tu  VamP 
phālgune vrīhayo mudgā vastrakṛṣṇājinādikam 
govindaprīṇanārthāya dātavyaṃ puruṣarṣabhaiḥ  VamP 
caitre citrāṇi vastrāṇi śayanānyāsanāni ca 
viṣṇoḥ prītyarthametāni deyāni brāhmaṇeṣvatha  VamP 
gandhamālyāni deyāni vaiśākhe surabhīṇi vai 
deyāni dvijamukhyebhyo madhusūdanatuṣṭaye  VamP 
udakumbhāmbudhenuṃ ca tālavṛntaṃ sucandanam 
trivikramasya prītyarthaṃ dātavyaṃ sādhubhiḥ sadā  VamP 
uvānadyugalaṃ chatraṃ lavaṇāmalakādikam 
āṣāḍhe vāmanaprītyai dātavyāni tu bhaktitaḥ  VamP 
ghṛtaṃ ca kṣīrakumbhāśca ghṛtadhenuphalāni ca 
śrāvaṇe śrīdharaprītyai dātavyāni vipaścitā  VamP 
māsi bhādrapade dadyāt pāyasaṃ madhusarpiṣī 
hṛṣīkeśaprīṇanārthaṃ lavaṇaṃ saguḍodanam  VamP 
tilāsturaṅgaṃ vṛṣabhaṃ dadhi tāmrāyasādikam 
prītyarthaṃ padmanābhasya deyamāśvayuje naraiḥ  VamP 
rajataṃ kanakaṃ dīpān maṇimuktāphalādikam 
dāmodarasya tuṣṭyarthaṃ pradadyāt kārtike naraḥ  VamP 
kharoṣṭrāśvatarān nāgān yānayugyamajāvikam 
dātvayaṃ keśavaprītyai māsi mārgaśire naraiḥ  VamP 
prāsādanagarādīni gṛhaprāvaraṇādikam 
nārāyaṇasya tuṣṭyarthaṃ pauṣe deyāni bhaktitaḥ  VamP 
dāsīdāsamalaṅkāramannaṃ ṣaḍrasasaṃyutam 
puruṣottamasya tuṣṭyarthaṃ pradeyaṃ sārvakālikam  VamP 
yadyadiṣṭatamaṃ kiñcidyadvāpyasti śuci gṛhe 
tattadvi deyaṃ prītyarthaṃ devadevāya cakriṇe  VamP 
yaḥ kārayenmandiraṃ keśavasya puṇyāṃllokān sa jayecchāśvatān vai 
dattvārāmān puṣpaphalābhipannān bhogān bhuṅkte kāmātaḥ ślāghanīyān  VamP 
pitāmahasya purataḥ kulānyaṣṭau tu yāni ca 
tārayedātmanā sārdhaṃ viṣṇormandirakārakaḥ  VamP 
imāś ca pitaro daitya gāthā gāyanti yoginaḥ 
purato yadusiṃhasya jyāmaghasya tapasvinaḥ  VamP 
api naḥ sa kule kaścid viṣṇubhakto bhaviṣyati 
harimandirakartā yo bhaviṣyati śicivrataḥ  VamP 
api naḥ santatau jāyed viṣṇvālayavilepanam 
sammārjanaṃ ca dharmātmā kariṣyati ca bhaktitaḥ  VamP 
api naḥ santatau jāto dhvajaṃ cakeśavamandire 
dāsyate devadevāya dīpaṃ puṣpānulepanam  VamP 
mahāpātakayukto vā pātakī copapātakī 
vimuktapāpo bhavati viṣṇvāyatanacitrakṛt  VamP 
itthaṃ pitṝṇāṃ vacanaṃ śrutvā nṛpatisattamaḥ 
cakārāyatanaṃ bhūmyāṃ khyaṃ ca limpatāsura  VamP 
vibhūtibhiḥ keśavasya keśavārādhane rataḥ 
nānādhātuvikāraiśca pañcavarṇaiśca citrakaiḥ  VamP 
dadau dīpāni vidhivad vāsudevālaye bale 
sugandhitailapūrṇāni ghṛtapūrṇāni ca svayam  VamP 
nānāvarṇā vaijayantyo mahārajanarañjitāḥ 
mañjiṣṭhā navaraṅgīyāḥ śvetapāṭalikāśritāḥ  VamP 
ārāmā vividhā hṛdyāḥ puṣpāḍhyāḥ phalaśālinaḥ 
latāpallavasaṃchannā devadārubhirāvṛtāḥ  VamP 
kāritāśca mahāmañcādhiṣṭhitāḥ kuśalairjanaiḥ 
paurogavavidhānajñai ratnasaṃskāribhirddaḍhai  VamP 
teṣu nityaṃ prapūjyante yatayo brahmacāriṇaḥ 
śrotriyā jñānasampannā dīnāndhavikalādayaḥ  VamP 
itthaṃ sa nṛpatiḥ kṛtvā śraddadhāno jitendriyaḥ 
jyāmagho viṣṇunilayaṃ gata ityanuśuśrumaḥ  VamP 
tameva cāgyāpi bale mārgaṃ jyāmaghakāritam 
vrajanti naraśārdūla viṣṇulokajigīṣavaḥ  VamP 
tasmāt tvamapi rājendra kārayasvālayaṃ hareḥ 
tamarcayasva yatnena brāhmaṇāṃśca bahuśrutān 
paurāṇikān viśeṣeṇa sadācāraratāñśucīn  VamP 
vāsobhirbhūṣaṇai ratnairgaubhirbhūkanakādibhiḥ 
vibhave sati devasya prīṇanaṃ kuru cakriṇaḥ  VamP 
evaṃ kriyāyogaratasya te 'dya nūnaṃ murāriḥ śubhado bhaviṣyati 
narā na sīdanti bale samāśritā vibhuṃ jagannāthamanantamacyutam  VamP 
pulastya uvāca 
ityevamuktvā vacanaṃ ditīśvaro vairocanaṃ satyamanuttamaṃ hi 
saṃpūjitastena vimuktimāyayau saṃpūrṇakāmo haripādabhaktaḥ  VamP 
gate hi tasmin mudite pitāmahe balerbabhau mandiraminduvarṇam 
mahendraśilpipravaro 'tha keśavaṃ sa kārayāmāsa mahāmahīyān  VamP 
svayaṃ svabhāryāsahitaścakāra devālaye mārjanalepanādikāḥ 
kriyā mahātmā yavaśarkarādyāṃ baliṃ cakārāpratimāṃ madhudruhaḥ  VamP 
dīpapradānaṃ svayamāyatākṣī vindhyāvalī viṣṇugṛhe cakāra 
geyaṃ sa dharmyaśravaṇaṃ ca dhīmān paurāṇikairvipravarairakārayat  VamP 
tathāvidhasyāsurapuṅgavasya dharmye sumārge pratisaṃsthitasya 
jagatpatirdivyavapurjanārdanastasthau mahātmā balirakṣaṇāya  VamP 
sūryāyutābhaṃ musalaṃ pragṛhya nighnan sa duṣṭāriyūthāpālān 
dvāri sthito na pradadau praveśaṃ prākāragupte balino gṛhe tu  VamP 
dvāri sthite dhātari rakṣapāle nārāyaṇe sarvaguṇābhirāme 
prāsādamadhye harimīśitāramabhyarcayāmāsa surarṣimukhyam  VamP 
sa evamāste 'surarāḍ balistu samarcayan vai haripādapaṅkajau 
sasmāra nityaṃ haribhaṣitāni sa tasya jāto vinayāṅkuśastu  VamP 
idaṃ ca vṛttaṃ sa papāṭha daityarāṭ smaran suvākyāni guroḥ śubhāni 
tathyāni pathyāni paratra ceha pitāmahasyendrasamasya vīraḥ  VamP 
ye vṛddhavākyāni samācaranti śrutvā duruktānyapi pūrvatastu 
snigdhāni paścānnavanītaśuddhā modanti te nātra vicāramasti  VamP 
āpadbhujaṅgadaṣṭasya mantrahīnasya sarvadā 
vṛddhavākyaiṣadhā nūnaṃ kurvanti kila nirviṣam  VamP 
vṛddhavākyāmṛtaṃ pītvā taduktamanumānya ca 
yā tṛptirjāyate puṃsā somapāne kutastathā  VamP 
āpattau patitānāṃ yeṣāṃ vṛddhā na santi śāstāraḥ 
te śocyā banadhūnāṃ jīvanto 'pīha mṛtatulyāḥ  VamP 
āpadgrāhagṛhītānāṃ vṛddhāḥ santi na paṇḍitāḥ 
yeṣāṃ mokṣyitāre vai teṣāṃ sāntirna vidyate  VamP 
āpajjalanimagnānāṃ hriyatāṃ vyasanormibhiḥ 
vṛddhavākyairvinā nūnaṃ naivottāraṃ kathañcana  VamP 
tasmād yo vṛddhavākyāni śṛṇuyād vidadhāti ca 
sa sadyaḥ siddhimāpnoti yathā vairocano baliḥ  VamP 
iti śrīvāmanapurāṇe aṣṭaṣaṣṭitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
pulastya uvāca 
etanmayā puṇyatamaṃ purāṇaṃ tubhyaṃ tathā nārada kīrtitaṃ vai 
śrutvā ca kīrtyā parayā sameto bhaktyā ca viṣṇoḥ padamabhyupaiti  VamP 
yathā pāpāni pūyante gaṅgāvārivigāhanāt 
tathā purāṇaśravaṇād duritānāṃ vināśanam  VamP 
na tasya rogā jāyante na viṣaṃ cābhicārikam 
śarīre ca kule brahman yaḥ śruṇoti ca vāmanam  VamP 
śraṇoti nityaṃ vidhivacca bhaktyā saṃpūjayan yaḥ praṇataśca viṣṇum 
sa cāśvamedhasya sadakṣiṇasya phalaṃ samagraṃ parihinapāpaḥ  VamP 
prāpnoti dattasya suvarṇabhūmeraśvasya gonāgarathasya caiva nārī naraścāpi ca pādamekaṃ śṛṇvan śuciḥ puṇyatamaḥ pṛthivyām 
 snāne kṛte tīrthavare supuṇye gaṅgājale naimiṣapuṣkare vā 
kokāmukhe yat pravadanti viprāḥ prayāgamāsādya ca māghamāse  VamP 
sa tatphalaṃ prāpya ca vāmanasya saṃkīrtayan nānyamanāḥ padaṃ hi 
gacchenmayā nārada te 'dya coktaṃ yad rājasūyasya phalaṃ prayacchet  VamP 
yad bhūmiloke suralokalabhye mahatsukhaṃ prāpya naraḥ samagram 
prāpanoti cāsya śravaṇānmaharṣe sautrāmaṇernāsti ca saṃśayo me  VamP 
ratnasya dānasya ca yatphalaṃ bhaved yatsūryasya cendorgrahaṇe ca rāhoḥ 
annasya dānena phalaṃ yathoktaṃ bubhukṣite vipravare ca sāgnike  VamP 
durbhikṣasaṃpīḍitaputrabhārye yāmī sadā poṣaṇatatpare ca 
devāgniviprarṣirate ca pitroḥ śuśruṣake bhrātari jyeṣṭhasāmne 
yattatphalaṃ saṃpravadanti devāḥ sa tat phalaṃ labhate cāsya pāṭhāt  VamP 
caturdaśaṃ vāmanamāhuragryaṃ śrute ca yasyāghacayāśca nāśam 
prayānti nāstyatra ca saṃśayo me mahānti pāpānyapi nāradāśu  VamP 
pāṭhāt saṃśravaṇād vipra śrāvaṇādapi kasyacit 
sarvapāpāni naśyanti vāmanasya sadā mude  VamP 
idaṃ rahasyaṃ paramaṃ tavoktaṃ na vācyametaddharibhaktivarjite 
dvijasya nindāratihinadakṣiṇe sahetuvākyāvṛtapāpasattve  VamP 
namo namaḥ kāraṇa vāmanāya nityaṃ yo vadenniyataṃ dvijaḥ 
tasya viṣṇuḥ padaṃ mokṣaṃ dadāti surapūjitaḥ  VamP 
vācakāya pradātavya gobhūsvarṇavibhūṣaṇam 
vittaśāṭhyaṃ na kartavyaṃ kurvan śravaṇanāśakam  VamP 
trisaṃdhyaṃ ca paṭhan śṛṇvan sarvapāpapraṇāśanam 
asūyārahitaṃ vipra sarvasampatpradāyakam  VamP 
iti śrīvāmanapurāṇe ekonasaptatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
iti śrīvāmanapurāṇaṃ samāptam
